Japan Reinforces Hankou. Japan Claims the Yoshioka Incident Occurred at Mei Foo Wharf. Our Side Discovers Eyewitnesses but Japan Refuses Consultation. Japanese Consul Miura Pays a Brief Visit to Yang Yongtai.

Hankou Dispatch: Regarding the case of the Japanese policeman Yoshioka being shot, it occurred within the Japanese concession, beyond the reach of Chinese political forces. Therefore, the Japanese authorities themselves must strive to investigate the case and arrest the perpetrators, while our government can only provide assistance under the principle of fostering friendly relations. However, observing the Japanese actions, including the landing of naval forces, police searches, erection of electric fences, meetings of officials and civilians, and reinforcement of troops to Hankou, all demonstrate their excessive tension. On the 21st, Japanese naval marines patrolled outside the concession twice with loaded weapons. On the 22nd, the destroyers "Ren" and "Mu" sailed from Shanghai to Hankou, carrying more than 200 naval marines, all anchored on the river in the Japanese concession, together with the originally anchored Ataka, Atami, Futami, and Katada ships, totaling six ships. Although the exact number of naval marines is unknown, it must be over 1,000 people. After the case occurred, the Japanese arrested Chinese hawkers, one being an old man and the other a child. The old man, Huang Qingyun, testified that he and the child Liu Ya's father set up stalls next to each other. On that day, Ya's father went to work at the Chinese wharf, instructing Ya to watch the stall. He heard two gunshots nearby and immediately went out to investigate, seeing the Japanese policeman fall to the side of the post from a distance, without seeing anyone fleeing. Although Huang is old, he feels his observations are more accurate than those of an eight-year-old child. However, the Japanese authorities seem to suspect that he was shot on the Chinese street and moved to the side of the post. After the Sino-Japanese joint trial the day before, today they requested the Municipal Government Secretary Zhang Xianghuai, Police Bureau Inspector General Wang Yufen, and Section Chief Dong Keren to consult, starting from 4:30 p.m. and ending at 6:30 p.m. At the same time, our Pacification Commissioner's Office and Provincial Government ordered the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters, Hankou Municipal Government, and Wuhan Police Bureaus to thoroughly investigate household registrations and examine suspicious persons. The Municipal Police Bureau also found several important eyewitnesses near the scene of the incident. The Municipal Government notified the Japanese side to send personnel to the Police Bureau for consultation at 3:30 p.m. on the 22nd. Because the Japanese personnel did not arrive, it had to be rescheduled, demonstrating the efforts of our authorities to assist. The Japanese Consul-General Miura has been meeting with Mayor Wu Guozhen for days to discuss assistance in the investigation. Today, the 22nd, he led two staff members across the river from Hankou to the Provincial Government to visit Chairman Yang Yongtai for a brief conversation. The content of the conversation is still unknown. However, the Japanese claim that the incident occurred not at the intersection of Nisshin Wharf and Dazheng Street, but near Mei Foo Wharf. As far as this reporter knows, in August of the Republic of China year 17, our four police departments set up posts in the area of Taikoo Dock and Yizi Street. The Japanese Police Chief Ogawa personally went to the branch bureau in charge and claimed that the area belonged to the Japanese concession, forcing us to withdraw the posts there. After several negotiations, when Liu Wendao was the head of Hankou in the 20th year, Police Chief Huang Zhenxing requested to consult with the Japanese Consul, stating that the public security management of the area was unclear and that bandits and communists could easily hide there, and that the police boundary line should be jointly measured and demarcated. The Japanese Consul replied that the boundary line there, that is, the line from the side of Sanxing Foreign Firm to the side of Taikoo Dock, including Taikoo Dock, forms a straight line, and there is no need for measurement, etc. These facts are only a few years old, and many people can testify to them. The government should also still have records. Therefore, the location of the incident, even if it is Mei Foo Wharf, is within the Japanese concession. (September 22nd)

Minnan Zhangzhou Area: Serious Bandit Disaster in Zhao'an. Meizhou and Xitan in Weiying Township are Occupied. Communists Burn and Loot, Losses are Huge. Sun Dingwen Launches a Large-Scale Suppression After Returning to Zhangzhou.

Xiamen Dispatch: The communist bandits Wu Jin, Yu Dingren, Yu Qitou, and others in Zhao'an County, Zhangzhou, are causing disturbances in Meizhou in the fourth district, Xitan in the third district, and Weiying in the second district, all of which are large townships with strong clans and resilient people with strong self-defense capabilities, long coveted by the communist bandits. Recently, Meizhou was attacked and occupied by Wu Jin and others, with more than 20,000 yuan looted and seven or eight village chiefs and wealthy households kidnapped. Except for five or six people who were redeemed, two are still in the bandit dens. Xitan was also occupied by bandits. Xitan was originally divided into upper and lower sections. The villagers in the upper section were incited by bandits and have mostly become bandits. The lower section suddenly felt weak in self-defense and was occupied by bandits. Several section chiefs were killed in this battle, dozens of rifles and short guns were looted, several houses were burned, the entire township was looted, and losses were no less than 100,000 yuan. Many people were also kidnapped and have not been released. The organization of the Baos, Jias and strong young men in Weiying was originally very strict, and it was not easy for strangers to infiltrate. The villagers are also brave and good at fighting. In view of the losses in Meizhou and Xitan, the security measures were strengthened. Every household in the township has guns. Those with money contribute money, and those without money contribute labor. They are also very united. At about 6 p.m. on the 15th, the communist bandits Wu Jin, Yu Dingren, and Yu Qitou jointly launched a sudden attack. The township reported to the Zhao'an County Government for help while dispatching strong young men to guard the key points in the township to resist. The two sides fought fiercely, and the artillery fire was very intense. After holding out until the morning of the 16th, the bandits used automatic rifles, machine guns, and Mauser pistols to cover the charge, and used homemade cannons to bombard, destroying all the wooden barriers and obstacles. The strong young men had no danger to defend and were captured. They still fought in the streets for a long time before retreating. The bandits then looted the entire township. The Zhou Battalion of the 80th Division stationed in the county seat rushed to support, and the bandits were preparing to retreat. The army pursued and captured three bandits, killed several, and confiscated four or five guns. In this battle, twelve strong young men were killed in battle, twenty-one were injured, and several guns were lost. In the afternoon, the army withdrew to the county seat, and the bandits returned to the township and looted it wantonly. Many villagers from Changpu, Shangyingzai, Shencuzhai, and Huxiangwei participated in the bandit party. The looting and destruction were extremely tragic, the losses were too great, and the people were terrified, and they moved to the county seat one after another. In addition, most of the villages in the second and third districts have become bandits, and the people are extremely afraid of bandits. They were coerced by the bandits, and the land has been distributed according to population in the Hunei area. The fields have been dug up and almost destroyed. Chen Qi arrived in Zhao'an on the morning of the 16th and took a special train to Zhangzhou. He agreed to the request of the party and government authorities and various agencies and social groups in Zhao'an to leave a battalion of Zhang Feiyuan temporarily stationed in Zhao'an, and then go after the relief troops arrived. In addition, Xikou Township in the second district of Shanghang, western Fujian, is close to the Yan Yong border. On the evening of the 11th, more than 100 bandits from Liao Haitao's troops suddenly came and fought fiercely with the strong young men until 3 a.m. on the 12th. Although the blockhouse was not breached, the bandits had entered the township and burned a large house of the Joint Guarantee Director Zhang Jingming's family and more than 20 households, killing 19 villagers, kidnapping more than 20 people, and looting tens of thousands of yuan worth of property. Chiang Ting-wen, Director of the Pacification Office in Fujian, returned to Zhangzhou from Guangdong on the 18th of this month, and summoned the division and brigade commanders to inquire about the recent bandit situation in western Fujian and Zhangzhou, and instructed on the suppression strategy. It was completed on the 21st, and the division and brigade commanders returned to their defenses separately and launched a large-scale suppression on the same day, which should be able to eliminate the bandits.

Li Zongren Returns to Guangxi. Withdrawal of the Weng Division Stationed in Beihai. Nanning Conference Begins to Handle the Aftermath in Guangxi. Guangdong Army Takes Over Beihai and Investigates the Nakano Case.

Li Zongren, Director of the Pacification Office in Guangxi, and Huang Xuchu, Chairman of the Guangxi Provincial Government, flew to Guangdong on the 17th to visit Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to ask for instructions on the aftermath of the Guangxi situation. After Li arrived in Guangdong, he and Chief of General Staff Cheng Qian, Chairman Huang Shaoxiong, and others formulated a plan for the aftermath of the Guangxi situation, discussed it in detail with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and discussed issues of concern to the two Guangdongs with the Guangdong military and political authorities. At 1 p.m. on the 19th, Li and Huang visited Chiang again. In addition to discussing the aftermath measures in Guangxi Province, they also discussed important national policies. Li and Huang retired at about 5 p.m. Li said that the Guangxi situation needed to be urgently returned to Guangxi to discuss and deal with Bai Chongxi, so he returned to visit Huang Musong, Chairman of the Guangdong Provincial Government, Yu Hanmou, Director of the Guangdong Pacification Office, and his old friends in Guangdong on the evening of the 19th. The next morning (the morning of the 20th), he took a plane back to Guangxi. Although Yu, Huang, and others wanted to host a banquet for Li that evening, it was too late. Li Zongren then took Huang Xuchu by car from Jiyuan, Dongshan to Tianhe Airport at 8:30 a.m. on the 20th. Those who saw him off included Ju Zheng, Cheng Qian, Qian Dajun, Yu Hanmou, Huang Musong, Xiang Hanping, Xu Jingtang and dozens of others. After Li and Huang got off the car, they exchanged greetings with the well-wishers, and then boarded the Junkers giant plane and headed west. All the well-wishers did not withdraw until the trace of the plane had disappeared. According to Li's statement to others before his departure, the results of this decision to come to Guangdong to visit Chiang Kai-shek were satisfactory. The number of troops in Guangxi Province has also been determined, and the military expenses will be subsidized by the central government every month. After Bai Chongxi has reorganized the troops, he can take up a new position. Another said that Li's hurried return to Guangxi was because the Weng Zhaoyuan's army in Guangxi had been stationed in Beihai for a long time and had not yet withdrawn. This move made it difficult to investigate the Nakano case, so the authorities urgently ordered Li to return to Guangxi to first withdraw the Weng's army stationed in Beihai in order to facilitate diplomatic progress. After Li arrived in Yongning, he convened a meeting with Bai Chongxi and others in Nanning to report on his visit to Chiang in Guangdong, and that the Guangxi army would be reorganized in accordance with the central government's establishment. It is heard that the Guangxi army will now be organized into divisions, with 20 regiments of soldiers, organized into six to eight divisions. The serial numbers will be listed as the Fifth Route Army, and Li Zongren will also serve as the commander-in-chief. The old troops of Cai Tingkai will be incorporated into the Guangxi army. After the establishment of the Fifth Route Army Headquarters, the former Fourth Group Army Headquarters and various district garrison commands of Guangxi Province will be revoked separately. As for Bai Chongxi's whereabouts, it has not yet been determined. It is expected that he will not be able to leave Guangxi until all the Guangxi army has been demobilized. After Li Zongren returned to Yongning, he immediately telegraphed the Weng Zhaoyuan's army stationed in Beihai to withdraw to the Guangxi border to await orders. The two division commanders, Weng Zhaoyuan and Qiu Zhaochen, then began to withdraw the troops stationed in Lianjiang, Hua County and Beihai on the 21st, and sent a telegram to Guangdong to report. The original telegram said, "Limited to arrival in Guangzhou immediately, General Commander Yu (Hanmou), Deputy Commander Xiang (Hanping), Staff Officer Xu (Jingtang), and Mr. Deng Yineng (Shizeng) were all informed. 1. The Hao telegram and Yi Gong's letter have been received. 2. Brother Zhuoyun has returned to Meiluo, and everything has been entrusted to him to convey. 3. The battalion of the Tan Division that took over Beihai has been asked to stop at Gongguanwei, and two officers will be sent to Beihai immediately to scout the position in advance. Tomorrow morning, Beihai will be handed over to the battalion to defend. This army also ordered the two division commanders, Tan Sui and Wu Jianhong, to advance from Gongguanwei to Lianjiang and Beihai on the 21st to take over the defense of the area. On the afternoon of the 21st, Weng Zhaoyuan's troops will be able to withdraw completely. As soon as the Fourth Route Army Tan Division is stationed in Beihai, Ling Tufen, the secretary sent by the Special Commissioner's Office for Diplomacy between Guangdong and Guangxi, will be able to land and conduct an investigation into the Nakano case and start negotiations with the Japanese side." (September 22nd)

Songjiang: Establishment of the Documents Committee

The county government of this county, upon receiving an order from the province, promulgated the organizational outline of the Municipal and County Documents Committee. In addition to the county's various bureaus and district chiefs as ex officio members as stipulated in the outline, County Magistrate Li also solicited opinions from all parties and invited local elders, scholars, and Confucian scholars as members, totaling 40 people. The establishment ceremony was held today, and the establishment meeting was held in the first building of Yunjian. The members who attended the meeting included Wang Zhewu, Shen Siqi, Min Ruizhi, Zhang Shutong, Lu Guiliang, Du Yizhi, and Sun Zongkun, etc. The ceremony was performed as scheduled. First, County Magistrate Li reported on the organization process in accordance with the order, followed by speeches by Wang Zhewu, Shen Siqi, and Lu Guiliang. Then the first regular meeting was held. Wang Zhewu was elected as the temporary chairman, and it was resolved to elect Lu Guiliang, Min Ruizhi, and Lei Junyan to draft the charter and rules of procedure of the association, Wang Zhewu to prepare the budget, and the annual operating expenses were limited to 400 yuan. Shen Siqi was immediately elected as the chairman. Then, the date of the monthly regular meeting was discussed, and it was decided to hold it on the 3rd and 17th of each month. A letter was also sent to the library to send the draft of the previous revision of the local chronicles to the association, and the county government and the county party headquarters were requested to instruct the district offices and their subordinate party headquarters to collect relevant documents, antiques, and records and send them to the association for safekeeping. At the same time, the status of various agency facilities was sent to the association for future inspection.

Nanhui: Four Robberies in One Night

The home of Cai Fuqing in Baiqu Township, District 9, was suddenly visited by seven or eight robbers with handguns the night before. They broke down the door and bound his entire family, robbing them of clothes and jewelry. That same night, the homes of Zhao Fuquan and a Mr. Chen in the Wangmiao area of the same district were also robbed of their property. Also, the home of Zhang Asheng, a worker at the Zhonghua Match Factory near Julong Bridge in the Beishi Town of the district, was also suddenly visited by eight robbers that night. Zhang tried to flee through the door, but was stopped by the robber's gun. Zhang ignored it and continued to run outside. The robbers, fearing exposure, rushed to hold him. Zhang struggled to break free and jumped into the river, and was forced to shore and bound. At the same time, the other robbers also bound Zhang's entire family, robbing them of cash, foreign clothing and other items before fleeing.

Taicang: A Frivolous Youth is Killed for Adultery

Shen Xingsheng, the son of Shen Yuqing, a farmer in Fangqiao Township in the county's third district, was only sixteen years old. He was frivolous by nature and did not work in the fields. Every day, he was only interested in seducing women. Yang A'quan's wife, a carpenter, was young and beautiful, and Xingsheng seduced her into adultery. They often met in secret. They continued their affair the night before, and were caught by the husband, who became angry and burned with anger. He took a sharp axe and chopped Xingsheng hard. He fled in pain, covered in blood, fearing being reprimanded by his father. He went to the river to wash his wound, but died on the ground due to excessive blood loss. Yuqing found out the story and reported it to the district office, which transferred it to the county for inspection. Shen Chengshen and Shen Chang carried the inspection officials and others to inspect.

Kunshan: Pedestrian Killed by Car

In the Xiao'anting area of the county's third district, a public car from the Shanghai Municipal Construction Association, traveling from Shanghai to Kunshan on the 21st, accidentally hit a pedestrian, Yang Shoulin, causing him to fall. He died from excessive bleeding from his head before he could be rescued. The villagers in the area reported it to the An'ting branch, which sent the police to detain the car and the driver Chen A'ming, and telegraphed the county government. After the personnel were dispatched for inspection, the first branch specially sent the car and the driver to the county for interrogation on the 22nd.

Aftermath of Drowning Case

Zhong Ahu, a farmer in Shage Village in the county's second district, drowned after getting drunk the day before. After the county's inspection confirmed the facts, he was coffined. Recently, the villagers in the area have been discussing and saying that Ahu was bound and beaten by police officers Zhang Licchun and Li Chenglin of the Public Security Patrol Office for causing trouble while drunk, causing his hands and feet to become numb. After being released, he fell into the river and died. His uncle, A'san, sued the county, accusing police officers Zhang Licchun and Li Chenglin of causing death by injury. On the 21st, the original defendants and related persons were summoned and interrogated. The police officers admitted to binding him lightly. The township chief Kong Ruifu was instructed to provide a written certificate, which will be investigated and verified.

Suzhou: Three Routes of Land and Water Bandit Suppression

Robberies and thefts have been frequently reported in various villages, and the bandit problem in Taihu Lake has resurfaced. Some days ago, the water police forces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces jointly suppressed the bandits in the Changbai Lake area bordering Jiangsu and Zhejiang. They encountered bandits opening fire in the Yangcheng Lake area, and the bandits abandoned their boats and fled. Now, the land and water public security authorities and the security team, in order to thoroughly suppress the bandits, jointly decided at a meeting to set out on three routes yesterday morning (23rd) for a large-scale joint suppression. The first route was the water police, led by District Chief Zhou as the commander-in-chief, leading the Anjing and Zhizhong warships and special teams, etc., which set out at 4 a.m. yesterday (23rd) and headed to Taihu Lake and the Yangcheng Dianshan lakes area to search and suppress. The second route was the seventh security brigade, consisting of the Gao Team Deputy Private Team Public Security Police Station and other three groups, which gathered in Xiangcheng yesterday morning and went to the villages of Tongjing and others to search and suppress. The third route was the Public Security Bureau, led by Director Zhang as the commander-in-chief, leading two shifts of the car patrol team and setting out on the Zhihe steamship. They gathered in Zhouzhuang and went to Jiaozhi Chenmu and other areas to carry out joint suppression yesterday morning, and ordered the garrisoned police teams to assist in the suppression, in order to connect all the land and water routes and annihilate the lake bandits.

Holding Air Defense Exhibition

The county party headquarters, the county government, the Public Security Education Bureaus, the Security Team, the Military Police Regiment and other six agencies, together with the Youth Association, will hold an air defense exhibition at the Youth Association from today (24th) to the 28th, displaying various models and paintings, etc., to educate the people, so that the people understand the importance of air defense. The significance is very important. After the ceremony was held at 9:00 this morning (24th), the exhibition began immediately, and leaflets were distributed and lectures were given on various broadcasting stations on certain days, in order to arouse the attention of the entire Suzhou public.

Wuxi: Tragic Death of Young Boss of Sauce Garden

Tao Zhonghou, the owner of the sauce garden and workshop of Bu Taochang outside the North Gate Wuqiao, is 68 years old. His wife, Mrs. Zhu, is about the same age. They have one son and four daughters. The son, named Zhaonian, is 30 years old and has one son and one daughter. There are more than ten branches in and out of the county, and the business is developed. In Wuxi, he can be called a wealthy man. However, the Tao family and his son are usually stingy, so there is very little contact with the outside world. In the afternoon of the previous (22nd), Zhaonian was riding a barge in the Beidiaochiao branch store, intending to go to the Wuqiao General Store. When the boat arrived at Jiangjiankou, a machine boat was driving towards it. Due to an accident, the two boats collided with each other. Zhaonian was standing at the bow of the boat looking at the scenery, and was knocked into the river and drowned. The machine boat was detained and negotiations were initiated. The body has now been salvaged. The Zhonghou couple were in tears and grief-stricken.

Widening of the Case of Beating a Rickshaw Puller to Death

The rickshaw puller Zong Xiaosizi accidentally bumped into the coppersmith Lian Linggen of the Arts and Crafts Iron Factory while pulling the rickshaw, causing him to be brutally beaten to death. After the court's inspection, there were two fatal injuries. The murderer, Lian Linggen, was taken into custody by the court. Yesterday, the Rickshaw Puller Union held an emergency meeting of the board of directors at the General Labor Union because Zong Xiaosizi died tragically. After deliberation, it was resolved that: (1) Personnel will be dispatched immediately to investigate the facts; (2) Based on the facts, a declaration will be drafted, requesting sympathy and assistance from all walks of life; (3) Appeal to the county party headquarters and consult with the local court's prosecutor's office to severely punish the murderer; (4) Send telegrams to the labor unions of all industries to jointly support the victims.

Court Promotion to First Class

The Ministry of Judicial Administration, considering that the county is located in the center of Beijing and Shanghai, is industrially and commercially developed, has a large population, and has a large number of lawsuits, has specially upgraded the local court to a first-class local court. In terms of the prosecutor's office, there will still be a chief prosecutor, who will be promoted by the current acting prosecutor Qian Chengjun. He has been issued a recommendation letter, ordering the Jiangsu Higher Court Prosecutor's Office to notify the local court prosecutor's office of the county. After receiving the order, Chief Qian specially issued a notice to the public for general knowledge. The vacancy of the prosecutor will be filled by the current candidate prosecutor Lu Qingfu. At the same time, the local courts of Nantong and Jiangdu counties have also been ordered to be upgraded to first-class local courts.

Changzhou: Tragic News of Couple Drowning

Shao Tingbiao of Wolong Town outside the West Gate of Wuyi was formerly a partner in a rice store, but is now unemployed. He married a Mrs. Gu and has one son and one daughter, the son named Fugen, 12 years old, and the daughter named Jujia, 14 years old, both studying in elementary school. Tingbiao used to be in love with a widow in a restaurant near Suoqiao, and has recently been living at the widow's place. In the afternoon of the previous day (21st), Tingbiao took his daughter Jujia to eat noodles at the widow's shop. Mrs. Gu heard the news and went to argue, causing a big conflict with Tingbiao. Then she returned home and continued to fight. After the neighbors persuaded her to stop, she suddenly burst into anger on the 22nd at midnight. The husband and wife fought again. Mrs. Gu was furious and rushed out the back door, jumping into the river to commit suicide. Tingbiao saw that the situation was not good and bravely chased after her, jumping in to save her. Mrs. Gu became flustered and grasped Tingbiao tightly. Tingbiao, although he knew how to swim, was unable to break free. Both husband and wife became the servants of the waves. After the wife's younger brother and others discovered it, they were salvaged. The two corpses were still embracing each other. Mrs. Gu was already seven months pregnant. The onlookers were horrified.

Changshu: Zhou Tongzhi Escorted to the Province

The county's telegraphic newspaper, for publishing personal news about the Security Team's soldiers, had its entire building destroyed on the night of the 5th of this month by Zhou Tongzhi, the leader of a division, leading the crowd. The group was shocked. The newspaper is temporarily operating from a fake inn office until the matter is resolved. Afterwards, the Security Command of Wuxi District sent personnel to Chang to investigate. The case has been reported to the Ministry, and the culprit of the incident, Zhou Tongzhi, has been escorted to Wuxi. However, Director Xiang of the Provincial Security Office attaches great importance to this matter. He ordered Commander Zang to escort Zhou to the province for verification, and ordered the county magistrate of the county to detain the accomplices in order to be strictly investigated.

Examination and Acceptance of Yangfu Road in Jian Ting

The Yangfu Highway in the county, which extends north to the Jiangbian area of Fushan and connects south to the Yangjian Station on the Xichang Road, has been completed after construction began in February this year. The provincial government specially dispatched Zeng Ding, and the Construction Bureau dispatched technician Wang Jiazhang to Changzhou on the 22nd to inspect the entire bridge and roadbed of the road from the engineering office. After inspecting each section, they were satisfied with the project. They returned to the province by car that evening. It is said that the right to operate the road will still belong to the Xihu Long-Distance Bus Company. Once the road surface is paved, it can be officially opened to traffic.

Nantong: Universal Establishment of Agricultural Warehouses

The Nantong County Agricultural Warehouse Management Committee held a meeting on the 22nd and decided that all eight agricultural warehouses already established in various rural areas will be universally established in areas where they have not yet been set up to regulate the rural economy.

Last month, the Baitan Farmers Bank agent office in this county was robbed of a large sum of money by bandits. Although the Security Brigade tried to investigate, it has not been solved. The bank transferred Yuan Shuren, the person in charge of the office, back to the Funing branch. Unexpectedly, Zhu, the deputy commander of the Yancheng District Security Command, came to Funing for inspection and learned that Yuan Shuren was suspected of colluding with Sun Houfu, Song Shaoqing, and others to rob the bank. After receiving the order, the team dispatched a team today to escort Yuan Shuren, Sun Houfu, Song Shaoqing, and three others to the Yancheng District Command for interrogation.

Jiaxing: Chamber of Commerce Requests Exemption from Household Tax

The Jiaxing County Government decided to levy household tax on the security group and household tax on shops at the same rate starting from the 25th year. However, the county's farmland has suffered from poor harvests, and the rural economy is bankrupt, resulting in the decline of all industries. Urgent government relief is needed, but even this may not be enough. If household taxes are levied again, it would be like adding insult to injury, and it would be impossible to accept. The County Chamber of Commerce and the Xinhuang and other town chambers of commerce have separately submitted requests to the provincial and county governments to cancel the household tax to alleviate the suffering of merchants and residents.

European Travel Correspondence: The "Conte Verde" Arrives in Hong Kong

— Xu Yu

From Shanghai to Venice is a journey of 30,000 miles. Traveling on the Italian-owned SS Conte VERDE, which holds world authority as a mail ship, takes 25 days. However, all advertisements promote travel to Europe in "23 days." It is true that it takes 23 days to get to Europe, but those of us who are traveling for the first time only think of Venice as our destination, so everyone mistakenly believes that we can get to Venice in 23 days. The ship weighed anchor at 4:00 PM on August 28th. I don't know if this has anything to do with the economics of advertising the date, but the departure time was set so early. Those who were seeing off passengers did not leave until two or three o'clock. When the passengers woke up, the ship was already at sea.

There were quite a few students on board this time who were going to Europe to study. There were probably 21 going to England, 18 going to Germany, 4 each going to France and Belgium, and 3 or 4 going to Italy. In addition, there were 5 or 6 couples going to work at the Chinese embassy in Italy. Besides that, there was one going to Austria and one or two going to Switzerland. These many Chinese children, whether they have done many things in society for many years, or have experienced much of life in China, or have just come out of university, whether they are on government scholarships or self-funded, are all children of the middle class or above. They all have a skill, and they can have a job in Chinese society. And everyone has a family. Why do they travel across the ocean to foreign countries? Whether it is for knowledge, fame, or profit, it is all for the sake of a bright future, and because they are dissatisfied with the current situation.

Almost all the students take second-class economy, but there are also passengers in the lower hold. In addition to Indians, the passengers are Chinese. Those Chinese are small merchants or craftsmen. Although they may not all be boarding the ship in Italy, they are leaving their hometowns for distant lands, and the various oppressions and hardships they suffer on the dock, on the ship, and in foreign lands far exceed those of the group of students. I once visited them a few days ago. The same place and berth, from Shanghai to Singapore, cost some people 75 yuan and others 35 yuan, a difference of such a large amount. People who don't know about it won't believe it, but friends who have traveled on Beiyang, Nanyang, and Yangtze River ships all know that to get to Tianjin or somewhere, the price of the same cabin can fluctuate by ten or so yuan, so there is nothing surprising about the high or low prices of ships here. There are countless hooligans in China who live by extorting money at the docks, and countless hooligans in the countryside who live by extorting money from the land. There are also countless people in education and politics... In short, if all the hooligans in China could obediently eat by working hard, there would be no traitors to sell the country and they would disappear. All unclear politics have an unclear group of people as a background, and they are mutually exploited. The function-style can only exist on one side. However, that group of small merchants and craftsmen still endure these thousands of deceptions and humiliations to go outside. Why is that? Isn't it still for the sake of seeking a bright future, because they are dissatisfied with the status quo and seek to move forward.

This shows that Chinese people are not unable to be dissatisfied with the status quo, and are not unable to seek progress, but they only seek individual improvement and have no collective resistance. The so-called individual improvement is a phenomenon that exists in the biological world. In the biological world, there are often changes in one's own physiological organization due to unsuitability to the environment. Collective resistance, on the other hand, changes the environment to suit one's own survival. This only exists in human society.

I am not saying that seeking individual improvement is an animal behavior. Individual improvement is also common among humans. Raising children can also be said to be individual improvement, and giving them education is also individual improvement. But the purpose of individual improvement in biology is to adapt to the environment, while in humans it is the opposite, it is to improve the environment. This is what makes humans superior to biological beings. However, there are not a few Chinese students who have returned to their country, and most of what we know is that they only adapt their individuals to the environment and engage in personal competition within the environment. Taking doctors as an example, there are thousands upon thousands of doctors in the cities, all of whom are capable students who have studied abroad, but they are all competing for business in the cities. There are very few who contact each other to change a small town or city into an environment with a scientific hospital! Taking education as an example, many, many capable students who have studied abroad only compete for positions, control, and squeeze others in the cities after returning. Who is willing to go to small cities and towns to run education and improve the educational environment? So, from these places, it can be seen that most Chinese people improve their individuals, can only adapt to the environment, and cannot improve the environment.

There are many Chinese people studying abroad who are good at their studies and have good knowledge. They go to foreign countries with great difficulty for the purpose of studying and improving themselves, so they often work harder than people from other countries, and their grades can also be above those of others. So, in terms of seeking individual improvement, Chinese people are not weak. So why can they only adapt to the environment after arriving in China, and cannot improve the environment?

This is because they lack collective organization and habits. Improving the environment requires this kind of organization and habits. It may not be possible for one doctor to run a hospital in a small town, but it is necessary to gather several doctors to be competent. The cultivation of this habit lies in the attention and connection during the process of individual improvement. Why do you study medicine abroad? You will definitely tell me that the equipment is good, the materials are good, and the organization is complete, so when you improve yourself, you must pay attention to improving the environment of your individual.

I once took a class from a Professor Zhou at the university. This professor was in charge of advanced psychological experiments, but he himself not only could not install the mechanical equipment for psychological experiments, but also did not understand it. As a result, many machines were only listed and not used. I think he may not have even seen these machines. However, when he was studying, he only did the experiment once on someone else's already installed frame, and of course he did not know anything about the experimental environment. People like this are not qualified to teach, but not paying attention to the environment is a common problem of Chinese people.

So, this is two-sided: individual improvement and new contact with group organization, understanding of the environment and transformation of the old environment. Among this group of travel companions, I hope they all have this awareness.

Local News

Gao Bingfang and Cui Weiwu Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday to Solicit Opinions from All Parties. Liang Jingchuan's Negotiations with the Banking Industry have been Successfully Completed. Gao Liang and Cui Attended the Mayor's Banquet in the Evening to Report on the Progress.

According to the Central News Agency, Liang Jingchuan, the deputy director of the Central Direct Tax Preparation Office of the Ministry of Finance, came to Shanghai a few days ago to discuss the procedures for securities, deposit interest, income, and income tax, and has reached a satisfactory result. It will be implemented on the 1st of next month on schedule, with Chinese and foreigners being treated equally. Gao Bingfang, the director, and Cui Weiwu, the secretary, also arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning to solicit opinions from all parties. The details are as follows:

Successful Negotiations

In order to equalize the burden on the people and adjust the state's tax sources, the Ministry of Finance, following the precedents of European and American countries, is implementing income tax and listing it as a central direct tax. Its regulations and detailed rules have long been passed and promulgated by the Legislative Yuan and the Executive Yuan, and it is scheduled to start on the first of next month, and the income tax on securities, interest, and income will be implemented first. The Shanghai banking industry stated that with the implementation imminent, various procedures are still waiting to be negotiated. After research by various banks, they made a statement to the preparation office, and Deputy Director Liang Jingchuan was dispatched to Shanghai to meet with the responsible personnel of various banks and explain in detail. The result was very satisfactory.

Mayor Hosts Banquet

Director Gao Bingfang and Secretary Cui Weiwu of the office also stated that with the opening of the new tax imminent, they must solicit opinions from all parties, so they came to Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning. After arriving at the station and checking into their lodgings, they went to the Municipal Government at about 10 o'clock to visit Mayor Wu for talks. In the evening, Mayor Wu and Fang Zhi, the acting Minister of the Central Propaganda Department, hosted a banquet for representatives of various newspapers at Xinghualou, and also invited Gao, Liang, and Cui to participate, introduced them to the members of the newspapers, and invited Peng Ge, the director of the General Propaganda Office of the Central Propaganda Department, to participate. Gao reported on the preparations for the collection of income tax.

Gao's Report

Gao rose from his seat at the banquet and reported, "Taking advantage of Mayor Wu's invitation to you today, and with the call of Minister Fang of the Central Propaganda Department, I will give a brief report on the progress of the preparation for income tax. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, there was a motive for implementing income tax, but it was not successful due to the instability of the political situation. After the Republic of China was rebuilt, the Beijing government decided to deliberate on the implementation in the first, third, fourth, ninth, and tenth years of the Republic of China, but it was also an empty promise and was not implemented, and it ended up being a flash in the pan. After the success of the Northern Expedition in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, the National Government prepared several resolutions, but because of the factual difficulties, it still had no end. It was not until July of last year that Minister Kong of the Ministry of Finance drafted a bill in accordance with the policies and political program of the Kuomintang of China, submitted it to the Executive Yuan for resolution, and sent it to the Legislative Yuan for review. This was considered to be the official start. The principles of income tax were passed by the Sixteenth Central Political Committee meeting on June 24th this year. The provisional regulations on income tax were passed by the Legislative Yuan meeting on July 9th. On July 21st, they were promulgated by the National Government. On August 18th, the 275th regular meeting of the Executive Yuan passed the detailed rules for the implementation of the provisional regulations on income tax. On August 22nd, the Executive Yuan announced these detailed rules. The legislative procedure for income tax is roughly like this. As for the content of the provisional regulations on income tax, it is based on the principles of fairness and simplicity, and takes into account the people's ability to pay taxes and the socio-economic conditions. Therefore, the currently set tax rate is extremely low, and the methods used are extremely simple. According to the scope of taxation promulgated in the provisional regulations, it is divided into three categories. The first category is income from profit-making businesses, which is calculated and taxed based on the net profit after deducting expenses. All companies, shops, firms, factories, or individuals with capital of more than 2,000 yuan are taxed on their profit-making income. Capital of less than 2,000 yuan is not collected. The income of government-private joint ventures and temporary profit-making businesses is taxed according to the amount of income in order to be fair. Moreover, the net profit of business income is less than five percent, or temporary income is less than one hundred yuan, and is still exempt from tax. The second category is salary income, which is taxed according to the salary income of civil servants, freelancers, and others engaged in various industries. Those who do not earn an average of 30 yuan per month are also not taxed. Moreover, the salaries of primary school teachers, and the pensions, disabilities, labor, and support funds for civil servants and officers who are injured or killed on duty, as well as the helpless, old-age pensions, alimony, etc., are all exempt from tax. The third category is income from securities deposits, which is taxed on the interest income from public bonds, corporate bonds, stocks, and deposits, calculated on the basis of each decision or settlement payment. The tax rate is no more than fifty per thousand, and the legal savings funds of civil servants and laborers, the foundation deposits of educational charitable organizations or groups, and educational savings funds are also exempt from tax if the annual interest income is less than one hundred yuan. According to the above classification taxation method, the net profit of the first category, profit-making business income, reaches five percent to one point, or the income is above one hundred yuan and up to one yuan, and only 30 per thousand of the net profit is levied. The tax rate for the second category, salary income, averages 30 yuan per month, and a tax of five percent is levied, which is lighter than that of other countries. The collection procedures are divided into two types: one is the method of withholding, such as the salaries of civil servants, which can be withheld by the salary-issuing agency, and the interest on bonds and deposits, which can be withheld by the interest-paying bank or savings association, etc. The second is the method of reporting, first by the taxpayer reporting themselves, and then by the government conducting random inspections and audits. This is the general situation of tax classification and tax rates. As for the progress of myself and my colleagues in preparing for income tax under orders, although there are no significant achievements to comfort everyone's expectations, I am very grateful for the enthusiastic support from all parties, and it has been very smooth and without encountering difficulties. In particular, I would like to thank the news media for their support in promoting the country. However, our office bears this responsibility, and is determined to follow Minister Kong's words: "We are determined to deal with new taxes with new talents and a new spirit." All the required staff will be recruited through examinations. In the first phase, 70 university graduates have been recruited and are now being strictly trained before being sent out to serve. At the same time, an accounting system will be established, and in the future, the collection and receipt of money will be handled separately and supervised by each other. No one can take advantage of loopholes or engage in malpractice. The collection costs will be minimized, and the handling procedures will be simplified. Regardless of the taxpayer, the method of choosing to be careless rather than disturb them is decided, so that they will naturally comply. We want to achieve a state of non-abuse, non-waste, non-panic, and non-disturbance in order to gain the sympathy of the people of the whole country. Foreigners are also treated equally, without any discrimination. Now, the 275th regular meeting of the Executive Yuan has resolved that, starting from October 1st of this year, the salary income of civil servants and the interest on bonds and deposits will be levied first, and the rest will be taxed again from January next year. Those of us in charge can only comply. The Ministry of Finance has now set up an income tax affairs office within the ministry to be responsible for collection affairs. Special commissioners have also been dispatched to various provinces and cities to contact local authorities in stages and handle matters related to the promotion of income tax. In the future, the central and provincial and municipal collection agencies will be based on this reasonable organization, and will gradually expand and improve it according to the needs of tax development and the training and development of talents. At present, the collectors are all incomes using the withholding method, so there is no need to expand the organization. This is the general situation of the preparation. Finally, I want to add that the theory of income tax, of course, everyone is very clear, and there is no need to repeat it. However, there are two very important meanings in coming to handle income tax this time. One is to reform the tax system. China's taxes have always been biased towards indirect taxes, and indirect taxes do not conform to the three principles of universality, fairness, and elasticity of taxes. More than 50 countries around the world that have implemented income tax all use income tax as the main pillar of their national tax revenue. There is absolutely no source that relies solely on indirect taxes, and there is absolutely no country that can become rich and strong without implementing income tax. If the country's finances are not on track, and the politics are not on track, there is no income tax. May I ask everyone, who can arbitrarily say that our country cannot go on the road to being on track? Moreover, since the foundation of indirect taxes is not solid, the country's financial resources, of course, cannot be relied upon as the foundation of taxes. Assuming that the country's situation changes, or the economic situation fluctuates, then indirect taxes will also be affected and unable to maintain the original amount of income. This situation is very likely to affect the stability of the country's finances, and may even shake the foundation of the country. Our country, which is in a precarious situation, must learn from past mistakes and open up a perfect path to establish a sound foundation for the country's finances in order to save the country and survive. This is the first saying. The second is to equalize the burden. We see that 80 percent of the country's population is farmers, and there are also many laborers. How are the burdens of this large group of farmers and workers? Their annual income is very small, but the direct and indirect burdens they bear each year are heavier than anyone else's. Everyone knows this unfair situation, and it can be said that they are suffering unbearably and cannot be saved. In recent years, the government has seen this, and the central and local governments have worked hard to cut and abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes, and want to change the situation, so that the burden of farmers and workers who are unable to pay taxes can be transferred to those who are able to pay taxes. In particular, this plan cannot be implemented without implementing income tax. If we do this, we can maintain the balance and coordination of people's livelihood, and we can equalize the obligation of the burden. The most important goal of equalizing the burden is the people's livelihood issue, and it is also to plan for national security. It is the only way to eliminate hidden dangers. For more than 20 years, the news media has always had the theory of saving the people's livelihood, and the news of the people's livelihood suffering has made the government vigilant day by day, and they have always loudly advocated and urged the government to reform and relieve the people's difficulties in the newspapers. Now it can be said that this decision to implement income tax is to realize the propositions of the news media and complete the goals of the news media. As for the current provisional regulations and methods, no one dares to arbitrarily say that they are perfect, because in our country it is still in its infancy, and it must be improved and progressed according to experience and facts. Talking about the responsibility of promotion, the government absolutely cannot give up its responsibility, and it is hoped that the news media will provide a lot of assistance and guidance. We must work together in order to achieve the long-standing hope of officials and civilians."

Gao's Talk

Gao met with reporters yesterday and said that the government has been preparing for the implementation of income tax for a long time. The consistent advocacy of the public opinion community has enabled the whole country to understand its significance and to implement it on schedule. He is very grateful. This tax is being implemented for the first time in our country, so various procedures need to be studied. Mr. Liang has had satisfactory results in his negotiations in Shanghai, and it will be implemented uniformly in Chinese and foreign banks across the country on schedule. As for foreigners, if there are any unclear points in the methods, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is explaining to various countries, and there will be no problems, he said.

Liang's Talk

Liang then told reporters that he had discussed with the banking industry in Shanghai and had detailed answers to the various procedural questions they had raised. The banks believe that there are no more problems and have decided to conduct a general settlement before implementation to clear the accounts. However, the branches in remote provinces are worried that various forms and other documents cannot be received on schedule and handled at the same time, and they have requested changes to avoid unexpected losses, which has been understood, he said.

Collection Procedures

Nanjing, 23rd, Central News Agency report: The Central Direct Tax Preparation Office of the Ministry of Finance will implement the first classified collection of income tax on October 1st. All income tax payments should be entrusted to the National Bank or the Postal Remittance Bureau for collection in accordance with the regulations of its implementation rules. The Director and Deputy Director of the Office, Gao Bingfang and Liang Jingchuan, are now going to Shanghai to sign a contract with the Three National Banks and the Postal Remittance Bureau for the collection of these taxes. The content of the contract is to stipulate that taxpayers should pay the first and second categories of income tax (not just referring to the income from public bond deposit interest) by self-payment, withholding, and proxy payment. If there is a Central Bank in the local area, it will be handed over to the Central Bank for collection. If there is no Central Bank, it will be handed over to the China and Communications Banks for collection. If there are no China and Communications Banks, it will be handed over to the Post Office for collection. As for the silver money industry, since it will be withholding deposit interest income on behalf of the government from October 1st, it needs to handle more settlement procedures. The authorities may give special rewards in the form of awarding bonuses.

Case of Japanese Sailors Shot: Around 8:20 PM Last Night, in Front of the Japan Shanghai Bank, One Person Died and Two Were Injured

Around 8:20 PM last night, at the corner of Wusong Road near Haining Road, in front of the Japan Shanghai Bank, three Japanese sailors were shot. One, a seaman first class named Tagang, was shot in the front chest, the bullet exiting from his back. Another, a seaman second class named Izuriha, was wounded in both arms. The third, a seaman first class named Yahata, was wounded in the right arm. In total, Tagang was shot twice, Izuriha twice, and Yahata once. After the incident, the patrol police immediately reported it to the Hongkou Police Station, which sent a vehicle to take the injured to Fumin Hospital for treatment. However, Tagang died shortly after arriving at the hospital due to his severe injuries. The other two sailors' injuries were not serious and they are expected to recover. They are currently still in the hospital receiving treatment. After the incident occurred, the police immediately began investigating the case. Lieutenant Ban Gu of the Japanese Marine Corps and the Japanese Consulate General also received reports and went to the scene to investigate. When the three sailors were shot, a public bus of route 2 happened to be passing by. It was suspected that the shots were fired from inside the bus, and the driver and ticket seller were once taken in for questioning. However, they were released after it was confirmed that they were not involved. After the incident, the police and Japanese Marine Corps soldiers jointly guarded the area and searched pedestrians. The area of the incident was heavily guarded. At the time of writing, the area was still under guard. During the search, a wooden-cased pistol was found in a yellow sand box placed by the Public Works Department at the intersection, and eight shell casings were found on the ground nearby. At the same time, three suspects were detained. After receiving the news, the Chinese police authorities paid great attention to the matter, fearing that the criminals would escape. They immediately ordered all police stations to send out all detectives to assist in the hunt, paying particular attention to pedestrians at the border between the Chinese and foreign concessions. Until late at night, in addition to the three suspects arrested earlier in Hongkou, who had been taken to the Marine Corps headquarters, there was no further development in the case, according to the Central News Agency. Four sailors from the Japanese warship Izumo were passing the Japan Shanghai Bank at the intersection of Haining Road and Wusong Road in the Public Concession at 8:20 PM on the 23rd, when they were suddenly attacked by gunmen. Seaman first class, Tagang Chaoguang, was shot through the chest and died on the spot. Seaman second class, Izuriha Zangji, and Seaman first class, Yahata Yoshiharu, were wounded in the arms. The other sailor was unharmed. The injured were sent to the Japanese Marine Corps Hospital on Jiangwan Road for treatment. After the incident, the concession police arrested a suspect near the scene and also found a pistol in a garbage can in a nearby alley. After receiving the report, the municipal government immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to assist in the arrest of the murderers and inspect pedestrians and homes in the area bordering the concessions. After the incident, the Japanese Marine Corps immediately dispatched troops to guard the area near the scene, inspect pedestrians, and patrol in armored vehicles, creating a tense situation.

According to a report from the Tongmeng News Agency in Shanghai on the 23rd, at approximately 8:23 PM tonight, near the Japan Shanghai Bank at the corner of Wusong Road and Haining Road, four Japanese sailors were walking when they were suddenly shot at by a Chinese person with a pistol. A total of eight shots were fired, hitting Seaman First Class Tagang in the chest. The sailor appeared to be attempting to reach the Zhicheng Japanese Bookstore around the corner, but died on the spot due to his injuries. Seaman Second Class Izuriha and Seaman First Class Yahata were also shot in the wrist. One of the assailants attempted to hide the pistol in a nearby sand box and was apprehended on the spot by a patrol officer from the Public Works Department. The others escaped. Detectives from the Japanese Marine Corps and the Hongkou Police Station rushed to the scene to investigate, prohibiting pedestrians from walking nearby. A rigorous search for the suspects was immediately launched, but the remaining accomplices have not yet been apprehended. According to eyewitnesses near the scene, the principal culprit appeared to be a Chinese man in Western clothing, aged 32 or 33, who fled towards North Sichuan Road after the shooting. Detectives from the police station recovered eight shell casings at the scene. A suspect arrested by the police station, a resident of No. 8 Xinruikang Lane, Dixiwei Road, was brought to the location for investigation by Lieutenant Ban Gu of the Japanese Marine Corps, Inspector Nakamura of the Public Works Department, Sergeant Shibuya of the Japanese Military Police, and representatives from the Japanese Consulate General.

A Reuters dispatch from Guangzhou on the 23rd reports that after news of the murder of a Japanese sailor in Shanghai arrived today, authorities here have taken various precautions to avoid any accidental incidents involving Japanese residents. The Municipal Standing Committee has issued a notice strictly prohibiting anti-foreign activities.

Sino-American Trade Association Held Regular Meeting Yesterday; Decided to Jointly Organize a Tourist Guide Association with Various Organizations

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the American Chamber of Commerce, the China International Trade Association, and the Chinese National Committee of the International Chamber of Commerce, in order to promote Sino-American trade, organized the Sino-American Trade Association last year. It was generally agreed that in various countries, special departments are set up or organizations are formed to promote and publicize tourism with tireless efforts. The income from foreign tourists exceeds tens of millions each year, which is a special income for various countries and can offset import surpluses. Moreover, it can promote culture and international understanding, which is of great benefit. Our country's famous scenic spots are renowned throughout the world, but due to the lack of systematic promotion abroad and the lack of organized guidance at home, European and American tourists abandon our country and go to neighboring countries, resulting in huge losses. It was decided to immediately join forces with various organizations to organize a Tourist Guide Association to conduct publicity and guidance activities, and to appoint committee members to investigate various inconveniences currently experienced by tourists visiting Shanghai and find ways to improve them. Outbound Competition on the Yangtze River; Large Quantities of Goods Blocked in Yichang; Shanghai Sichuan Merchant Groups Greatly Alarmed

Due to the crowding of goods for shipment, freight rates for various Sichuan River shipping companies are rising. For cotton yarn shipped from Shanghai to Chongqing, the lowest freight rate was only three yuan per piece, but it has now risen to eighteen yuan, an increase of six times. With the Upper Yangtze River expected to become shallow soon, freight rates are expected to rise further. It is said that there are discussions to increase rates by another two yuan per piece starting on the first of next month. According to people in Sichuan merchant groups, during the dry season this year, if freight rates continue to increase at this rate, the freight rate for cotton yarn could reach twenty-six yuan per piece. For foreign goods (which are actually domestic goods, such as galoshes, toothbrushes, enamelware, blankets, and towels), the rate is also around one hundred yuan per ton. Therefore, the Sichuan River shipping industry is better than any other shipping route. Currently, the shipping companies operating on this route include Minsheng, Taikoo, EWO, and Nissin, which are all listed as regular liner services on the Yangtze River. According to the Ministry of Transportation's restrictions, non-regular liner services are not allowed to operate on this route, so the allied companies are protected in their business and do not have to worry about ships outside the alliance competing with them. Two months ago, the Shen'ai, a foreign-flagged ship managed by the Yilong Foreign Firm in Shanghai, suddenly changed its route from the Northern Seas to the Upper Yangtze River to compete for Shanghai cargo bound for Sichuan. Because it had a deeper draft and larger hull, it was able to ship heavy cargo directly from Shanghai to Yichang. It then transshipped the cargo onto smaller Sichuan-bound boats for transport upriver. Because the freight rates were cheaper, many customers were eager to use it, and every shipment was fully loaded. The allied companies did not initially pay attention, but recently realized that this move would harm the Sichuan River shipping industry and greatly impact the outgoing goods and freight rates. The companies held a meeting to discuss countermeasures and decided to take a passive resistance approach: all Sichuan-bound boats from the allied companies would refuse to transship goods that had been transported to Yichang by the Shen'ai, so that the goods would be permanently blocked in Yichang and unable to reach Chongqing. This plan was implemented when the Shen'ai arrived in Yichang for the third time. It is said that there are now thousands of pieces of cargo blocked in Yichang, worth hundreds of thousands of yuan. Yichang has sent urgent telegrams to Shanghai. Many Sichuan merchant groups in Shanghai have goods blocked in Yichang. With the Mid-Autumn Festival approaching, the blockage of goods has brought financial activities to a halt. The various groups held a general meeting at the Sichuan Department Store Mutual Aid Association in Shanghai to discuss solutions. As a result, the mutual aid association sent a letter to the shipping companies, requesting them to quickly transship the goods and not allow hundreds of thousands of yuan of goods to be blocked. The original letter was very long and is not reproduced here. If this measure is ineffective, it was decided to appoint representatives to negotiate with the shipping companies in person. The companies have not yet expressed their attitude. It is difficult to predict what will happen in the future. The situation is quite serious. Since this incident, customers have become wary of using non-regular Sichuan River ships. As a result, foreign-flagged ships operating on this route may suspend their operations.

Returned Goods Unable to Obtain Shipping Permits Again: Woolen Fabric Guild Announces Refusal of Returns

In order to prevent smuggling, the central government has issued a decree requiring goods to obtain a shipping permit before they are allowed to be transported. The Woolen Fabric Guild of this city has announced that goods may not be returned thereafter, as customer groups in various locations often return goods, making it impossible to obtain permits again. The announcement is recorded below:

"Since the implementation of anti-smuggling measures, it has been necessary to obtain shipping permits from the Customs for all transported goods, and the quantity of goods to be transferred has been noted on the original permit. This has been followed uniformly. However, recently, various member firms have reported that customer groups in various locations, after selecting and accepting goods and completing all the necessary shipping permit procedures, suddenly claim that the goods are not as described or use the excuse of sluggish sales to return the goods. The original seller finds it difficult to restore the original state of the permit with the Customs. As the returned goods have lost their permit basis, they cannot be resold, resulting in significant losses. They have requested that restrictive measures be put in place. After investigation, once goods have been selected, inspected, and accepted, and a contract has been agreed upon, there is no reason for returns. To eliminate all disputes, the council has now decided that after customer groups select and receive goods, and the consignee fills out and stamps the shipping permit, no returns will be allowed under any circumstances. This is hereby announced in the newspaper for public knowledge."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River Transport: Results After Rectification, Using Passenger Revenue as a Comparative Standard, Income Has Increased by More Than 15%

During the comprador system period, all personnel administration and passenger revenue of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River vessels were handled by the business director. The company only collected a fixed amount from the business director each month according to the stipulated ratio. On April 1st of this year, in order to rectify operations and increase revenue, the company abolished the comprador system for all Yangtze River vessels and changed to a system of actual reporting and reimbursement. All personnel administration was directly managed by the company, and all passenger revenue was handed over to the company. On the other hand, the company strictly investigated passengers traveling without tickets, strictly prohibited tea room staff from soliciting tips, improved vessel facilities, and implemented armed escorts. Since implementation, there has been significant progress in improving the convenience and comfort of passengers and maintaining the order and cleanliness of the wharves.

Therefore, the Jiangshun, Jiang'an, Jianghua, Jiangxin, Jiangda, and Jianguo vessels on the Shanghai-Hankou line have seen an increase in passenger revenue even though ticket prices remain the same. From April to July of this year, the total revenue from first, second, third, fourth class, and other passenger tickets was 266,149.21 yuan. After deducting administrative expenses (formerly borne by the compradors, now paid by the company) of 100,597.65 yuan, the net profit was 155,525.46 yuan. Compared with the total fixed amount during the comprador period of 134,468 yuan, the net profit increased by 21,097.46 yuan in four months, accounting for 15.66% of the income during the comprador period. Currently, passengers on most Yangtze River vessels using the comprador system must pay extra for berths and large tips in addition to purchasing tickets, with the total amount nearly equal to the ticket price, which is very uneconomical. Therefore, many passengers choose to travel on the company's vessels. Unfortunately, the company does not have enough vessels to meet the demand. Recently, the company and its branch offices along the Yangtze River have experienced extreme crowding of passengers booking cabins and purchasing tickets before each vessel arrives at the port, and supply cannot meet demand. The company regrets that it cannot meet the needs of its customers.

Forging Loan Documents and Extortion: Gu Pingzhen and Others Sentenced

The wealthy elderly widow Ms. Yin, residing in Xicang Bridge in the city, was recently sued in the local court by Gu Pingzhen, a Baoshan native who runs the Baoli Hosiery Factory, for a loan of 100,000 yuan and interest of 10,000 yuan. Gu claimed that in 1920, Ms. Yin, with her eldest son-in-law He Shuhe (the owner of the bankrupt Xiaodongmen He Hengchang Silk and Satin Shop) as guarantor and her other son-in-law Cheng Qizhi (an employee of Samsung Jewelry) as intermediary, borrowed the money from Gu's grandmother, Gu Gongshi. Before her death, Gu Gongshi entrusted the loan to Gu, hence the request for repayment.

However, Ms. Yin stated that she had never met the Gu family and had no financial dealings with them. She also claimed that she was quite wealthy and would not have needed to borrow money in 1920. She also stated that she used to give each of her sons-in-law 50 yuan per month, but recently stopped the payments due to tenant rent arrears and vacant houses, which angered them. Additionally, the Yongji Company house in Tianxi Lane, Zhengjia Bridge, was entrusted to Cheng Qizhi to collect rent, but since the end of last year, the task was transferred to Lawyer Xu. Cheng Qizhi refused to hand over all documents. After mediation by relatives and friends, he handed over the documents after being paid 1,700 yuan. Three days later, this lawsuit arose. Therefore, she hired Lawyer Fang Junjie to file a lawsuit in the criminal court against Gu Pingzhen, He Shuhe, and Cheng Qizhi for forging private documents with the intent to defraud. Judge Wu Xiangzu suspended the hearing. The defendants hired Lawyer Wu to defend them. Gu Pingzhen, He Shuhe, and Cheng Qizhi were initially detained. Cheng was later released on bail with a large guarantee from his employer, Samsung Jewelry. Gu and He remained in custody.

The plaintiff presented Gu Pingzhen's uncle, Gu Wenhua, as a witness, who testified that his mother, before her death, only instructed her descendants to be cautious and not to tarnish the family's reputation, and never handed over any loan documents. Furthermore, the judge had calligrapher Wang Xishen authenticate the loan document. The handwriting was similar to that of He Shuhe. An investigation also revealed that the stamp on the loan document, as verified by the city chamber of commerce, was from 1933. The case was thus clarified, and the debate was declared closed. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu held a court session and sentenced Cheng Qizhi in absentia. Gu Pingzhen and He Shuhe were brought to the court, and after briefly questioning their ages and backgrounds, the judge read out the verdict: Gu Pingzhen was sentenced to two years of imprisonment for jointly forging documents with the intent to illegally possess property and to harm the public or others. He Shuhe and Cheng Qizhi were each sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment for the same actions. After the verdict, the defendants and their lawyers requested that Gu Pingzhen and He Shuhe be released on bail, but the judge denied the request and ordered them to be returned to custody. The defendants immediately announced their intention to appeal and hired Lawyer Sha Xunyi to handle the appeal to the higher court of the second instance.

Robbers Unsuccessful in Robbery: Shot and Killed an Indian Constable, Robbers Jumped into Yu Songjun's Car and Speeded Away on a Escape Run

At around 10 AM yesterday, three robbers suddenly entered the home of Dr. Liu Yixiang, an ophthalmologist residing at No. 6 Maurice Villas on Racecourse Road, and attempted to rob the place with guns. Liu, seeing the intruders' ill intentions, immediately fled to the third floor and took refuge in No. 8 next door. Liu's wife tightly closed the door to the third floor and shouted "Catch the robbers!" from the window facing Racecourse Road. The robbers, realizing the situation was unfavorable, did not dare to act and turned to flee eastward.

At that time, Constable No. 189, stationed at the intersection of Mohawk Road, had heard the alarm and rushed over. Seeing the three robbers coming towards him, he bravely stepped forward and grabbed one of them. The other two robbers, seeing their accomplice being arrested, immediately fired their guns, shooting Constable No. 189 in both shoulders and chest. He fell to the ground, wounded. The captured robber also managed to escape. The other two robbers fled towards the Xiaocai Market on Dagu Road, passed through Rue Edouard VII, crossed Rue de Tientsin, and reached Avenue Foch. By this time, the French Concession police had received the information and were closely pursuing the robbers.

In their panic, the two robbers suddenly saw a car parked in front of No. 145 Avenue Foch. Without asking any questions, they opened the car door, forced the occupant out of the car, jumped inside, and ordered the driver at gunpoint to drive west. The driver had no choice but to obey. At the same time, the two robbers fired two more shots at the pursuers from the car. After the car passed Rue Petain and Rue de l'Eglise and reached the front of Tongde Pawnshop at No. 83 Rue du Pere Froc, the two robbers finally ordered the car to stop, jumped out, and fled west. The car driver, unable to think of any other solution, turned the car back to Avenue Foch and reported the incident to the French police station.

It was then learned that the car belonged to obstetrician Yu Songjun. He was on his way to pick up a female doctor to assist in a delivery at No. 11 Route des Soeurs when the robbers hijacked the car. The injured constable died from his wounds. His body was transferred to the Chinese Police Hospital. The police are preparing a grand funeral for him and have ordered all personnel to cooperate in the arrest of the escaped robbers.

Mao A'gen, driver of the No. 650 car at the Xinzha Fire Station, Jiang Yuanying, firefighter No. 231 at the Central Fire Station, and Lin Gendi, a waitress at the Xianshi Amusement Park, are suspected of jointly killing Cai Ying, a waitress at the Daxin Amusement Park, at No. 3 Cunfu Lane, Baobao Road, on August 9th, dismembering her body, and abandoning it. The case is under investigation by Huang Fusen, Liu Zhaonian, Chen Defu, and Deng Shu, detectives of the Hongkou Police Station, who arrested Mao and others and sent them to the First Special District Court for repeated interrogations, as previously reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Zhong Qing of the First Special District Court continued the hearing in the third criminal court. The men and women in the audience were extremely crowded.

The large third criminal court was nearly impossible to stand in, and many people were excluded from the courtroom. Since the court adjourned the hearing, Mao A'gen has confessed everything to the police. He stated that they had agreed beforehand to start from the Xinzha Fire Station on the 9th. After killing Cai Ying, Gendi bought a reed mat and put the head in it. Then he used a blanket to wipe away all the blood. After dismembering the corpse, he put it in the box and locked the door. They then went out together. That evening, Mao and Lin went to the Zhonghua Xieji New Hotel at No. 387 Avenue Avener and opened room No. 31, writing "No. 690, 32 years old, patrolman" in the register. At 6:45 AM on the 11th, they went to Cunfu Lane.

Took the box out
