Executive Yuan Responds to National Goods Association: Raincloth Should Reduce Costs, The Way to Compete with Foreign Goods, Increasing Import Tax Rates is Pending

The China National Goods Maintenance Association, at the request of the Lianpu Waterproof Fabric Factory, presented documents to the National Government, Executive Yuan, Ministry of Finance, and Ministry of Industry on June 26, requesting that all agencies be ordered to use domestic raincloth and increase import tax rates on foreign raincoats and fabrics to promote national goods. The association received a reply from the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, No. 6693, stating: "The President has ruled that the case of the China National Goods Maintenance Association's request to increase import tax rates on foreign raincoat fabrics should be reviewed by the Ministry of Finance, and the original presenters should be informed." Accordingly, a copy of the original document is enclosed for your reference. Addressed to the China National Goods Maintenance Association. Enclosed is a copy of the original letter from the Ministry of Finance. Secretary-General Weng Wenhao of the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan.

The original letter from the Ministry of Finance states: "Received letter No. 5009 dated July 6, this year, opening with 'The President has ruled that 'the China National Goods Maintenance Association presented on June 16th of the fifteenth year, to distinguish between domestic raincoats, paintcloth, and other products and non-domestic goods, requesting that all agencies thoroughly investigate merchants who cover up and use foreign goods to impersonate domestic goods, hindering the development of domestic goods, ordering the use of domestic products, and increasing the import tax rates of foreign raincoats and fabrics to promote them, should be submitted to the Ministry of Finance and Industry for review and instructions be issued.'' In addition to the President's instructions and separate letters, a copy of the original document is enclosed for your reference." Regarding the original request to increase the import tax rates on foreign raincoat paintcloth, the Mountain National Tariff Committee has been instructed to investigate and review it. After further review, the Ministry found that the lowest market price of foreign cotton raincoat fabrics in Shanghai is 4 Jiao per unit, and the cost is at most 2 Jiao per unit. The cost of domestic goods is nearly 1 Jiao per yard for the blank fabric, and at least 3 Jiao for processing, totaling 5 Jiao. Comparing the two, the price of each yard differs by 1 Jiao. It is clear that domestic raincoat fabrics will not be able to compete with foreign goods unless they strive to reduce costs in manufacturing. The import tax rate for foreign raincoat fabrics is currently levied at 25% ad valorem. The request to increase the tax rate should be considered when the tariff is revised in the future. With the approval of the previous letter, we hereby reply to your office for reference and submission. Addressed to the Secretariat of the Executive Yuan, Kong Xiangxi.

Assassination of Shao Wenbin Case: Two Suspects Claim Frame-Up, Firmly Deny Charges Despite Court Confrontation, Ordered to be Held in Detention Center for Rescheduled Trial

Shao Wenbin, the "Flower Association King" from Pudong, also known as "Driver Sixth," was shot and killed on the evening of July 28, 1933, at the intersection of Avenue Wagner and Rue de la Mairie in the French Concession. Subsequently, the French police arrested the suspect, Zhang Bingrong, a Ningbo native nicknamed "Little Ningbo," and handed him over to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. The initial trial sentenced him to 15 years in prison, but the High Court's Third Branch overturned the verdict and sentenced him to life imprisonment. During the trial, Zhang confessed that Wang Shilong, who was at large, had conspired with him to carry out the assassination. The court issued an arrest warrant for Wang Shilong, and he was finally apprehended by the French police and handed over to the Second Special District Court.

Custody and Investigation

According to the case file, during the investigation, Wang confessed to accomplices Qian Ajin and Ma Pi Ajin. Qian was also arrested, and the cases were merged for investigation. This has already been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Judge Wang Gangxu of the Second Special District Court, accompanied by clerk Gao Yan, conducted a preliminary hearing in the First Criminal Court. Attorney Gu Shouxi from the Police Department presented the case, stating that the Police Department was now prosecuting the defendants Wang Shilong and Qian Ajin under Article 271 of the Criminal Law for murder, and Articles 267 and 268 for intent to profit and engaging in illegal flower association gambling. He stated that after the victim, Shao Wenbin, was assassinated on the evening of July 28, 1933, the police

Arrested the Murderer

Zhang Bingrong, who was sentenced to life imprisonment by the court. According to Zhang's confession, Wang Shilong had arranged a meeting at the Yuebin Hotel to discuss the plan, inviting Zhang Bingrong, Li Landi, Si Gen, Chen Changgeng, and others to kill Shao. Wang also discovered that Shao passed by Rue de la Mairie and Avenue Wagner every evening after leaving the Far Eastern Hotel. On the evening of July 28, they carried out the murder. Now Wang has confessed to the assassination in the police station and implicated Qian Ajin, requesting that they be interrogated according to the law. Wang Shilong and Qian Ajin both denied participating in the conspiracy to assassinate Shao Wenbin and claimed they did not know Shao. Wang also claimed he had a feud with Zhang Bingrong because Zhang had sent him an invitation, and when he didn't send a gift, Zhang demanded the invitation back.

Verbal Quarrel

He hit me, and I held a grudge and bit him. I did not participate. My confession at the police station was only due to unbearable suffering. I confessed nonsense. Qian claimed that he did not confess to participating in Shao's murder at the police station, only admitting to being a lookout for the flower association, but stopped when he didn't get paid. Now he is being falsely accused. Both defendants hired Wu Kaisheng, Huang Xiubo, and Wang Shou'an as their lawyers. The court wanted to present Zhang Bingrong as a witness, but it was already near noon, and there was no time for questioning. The hearing was adjourned until 2 p.m. In the afternoon, at 3 p.m., Judge Wang continued the trial at the Criminal Court and first questioned the witness Zhang Bingrong, who testified that he had not participated in the assassination of Shao Wenbin.

Wrongful Arrest

Sentenced to life imprisonment. I knew Wang Shilong before. He asked me to go to the Chunjiang Hotel and meet Chen Changgeng. Chen recommended me to work as a tea server at Cao Awu's house. At Cao's house, I heard Cao Awu, Zhao Liansheng (Cao's son-in-law), Li Landi, and another person I didn't recognize discussing killing Shao Wenbin. Wang Shilong was not present. I did not know Qian Ajin either. Later, Chen Changgeng told me that he, Li Landi, Si Gen, Xiao Mao, and others had gone to kill Shao because of

Robbing Flower Associations

I have no deep hatred for Wang Shilong, but reflecting back, I was arrested because I met Wang Shilong. He asked me to go to the Chunjiang Hotel and meet Chen Changgeng, who asked me to work as a tea server. That's why I implicated Wang Shilong. The court then questioned Wang Shilong and Qian Ajin again, who still vehemently denied killing Shao. After repeated confrontations, Wang and Qian continued to deny the charges. As a result, the court ordered a postponement until October 1 for further interrogation. The defendants were ordered to be held in the detention center.

Shanghai West Civic Education Experimental Zone: Training Model Rickshaw Pullers, Imparting Basic Knowledge, Correcting Behavioral Errors

The Shanghai West Civic Education Experimental Zone, recognizing that most rickshaw pullers have not received adequate education, which sometimes leads to unreasonable behavior, is launching a training program for model rickshaw pullers to eliminate negative attitudes. Yesterday, the first training session was held at the General Counseling Office on Zhongshan Road. The event was very enthusiastic. The details are as follows:

Crowded Attendance

Yesterday afternoon, Director Tang Mao of the zone, Director Ling Zhiying of the Rural Department, Director Xu Shuquan of the Urban Department, Counselor Lou Jiaji and staff Zhou Congyi of the Twenty-Second Community of the Xujiahui District, and over fifty hardworking rickshaw pullers, including Qu Chunlin, Xue Hongshan, Wu Huanchun, Zhu Zengtai, Qu Fengqi, Sha Changchun, and Jiang Dengshan, attended the training session. Under the direction of Urban Department Director Xu Shuquan, the training began as the sun set. Discipline was strictly enforced.

Preliminary Training

(1) Training on Meeting Procedures: A. Singing the Party Song, B. Saluting, C. Reading the Will, D. Silent Meditation; (2) Basic Civil Rights: A. Proposals, B. Explanations, C. Discussions, D. Voting; (3) Mutual Teaching and Learning: A. Men and women, young and old, love each other, B. Relatives, neighbors, and friends, help each other, C. Building roads benefits everyone, D. Cleaning up filth serves the public. Following this, the directors of each department delivered speeches. The meeting ended around 9 p.m.

Summary of Speeches: (1) Director Tang Mao of the zone delivered a speech, stating: "Chinese people only know how to eat, work, and pursue their own happiness, and are unwilling to cooperate with others for common benefit. Now we must 'cooperate to survive.' We must organize the Twenty-Two Communities, implement joint management under the principle of cooperative production, improve the lives of the masses, and achieve the goals of 'everyone doing their best,' 'everyone enjoying the fruits of their labor,' 'everything being used to its full potential,' and 'everything yielding its benefits.' So, how can one be a member of the Twenty-Two Communities? As long as one has (1) sound character, (2) a spirit of cooperation, (3) abundant knowledge, and (4) good habits, one can be a community member and a good community member is a good citizen. Therefore, if a person can understand the meaning of 'cooperation' and the relationship between 'people and people,' it will be easy to follow the twelve covenants below: (1) Wear homespun cloth, (2) Use domestic goods, (3) Do not smoke, (4) Do not gamble, (5) Work diligently, (7) Spend frugally, (8) Do good deeds, (9) Love cleanliness, (10) Value hygiene, (11) Be friendly to neighbors, (12) Help each other." (2) General Director Lou spoke on "Model Rickshaw Puller Guidelines," stating: "A model rickshaw puller is one whose words and actions can serve as an example for other rickshaw pullers. Of course, a perfect model rickshaw puller cannot be achieved immediately, so we have temporarily stipulated a few points: (1) Be able to comply with the covenants stipulated by this zone, and be confirmed by the zone's investigation; (2) Receive the most votes in the model rickshaw puller general election; (3) Be confirmed as good by local police officers and passengers." B. The Creation of Model Rickshaw Pullers: (1) Performance in fulfilling covenants accounts for 50%; (2) Election votes account for 30%; (3) Social evaluation accounts for 20%. C. Rights of Model Rickshaw Pullers: (1) The right to request small loans from this zone; (2) The right to request treatment, introduction to treatment, and learning treatment from this zone; (3) The right to request assistance with legal matters from this zone." D. Obligations of Model Rickshaw Pullers: (1) The obligation to obey all orders of this zone; (2) The obligation to guide and report the lives and behaviors of other rickshaw pullers; (3) The obligation to implement the zone's pre-set covenants and various collaborations, and to serve as a model for other rickshaw pullers." (3) Director Ling of the Rural Department spoke on "Methods from Rickshaw Pulling Cooperation to Animal Husbandry Cooperation," stating: "Rickshaw pulling is too simple, and life is very difficult. We should utilize the free time of housewives and children to adjust family work and increase production. Animal husbandry in the family should focus on livestock that are easy to raise and produce a large yield, such as Angora rabbits, chickens, and ducks. If this is organized with the funds of all the members, it will definitely achieve twice the result with half the effort."

Public Concession to Have Two Parking Lots, Municipal Council to Set Up Free Parking Lot

According to a translation of a mainland newspaper by a foreign news agency, before the implementation of the Municipal Council's new parking regulations on October 15, Shanghai will have two large parking lots. It is also rumored that a real estate company plans to open a third parking lot. One will be located between Fuzhou Road and Henan Road, at the former site of the Central Police Station, which will be leased by the Municipal Council to a business for operation, and a small portion will be set aside for a gas company to set up a branch. The second will be located between Central Road and Xinkang Road, operated by the Shanghai Land Company. The monthly rent for the first lot will be about five to eight yuan, and the rent for the second lot will be seven yuan for cars and three yuan for chartered cars. The first lot was put out for lease in August, and three companies have submitted bids. The decision will be made soon, and the parking facilities should be completed by October 15. The first lot will have space for 90 vehicles, and it is expected to be ready in early October. It is said that half of the spaces have already been reserved by car owners. In addition, the company will hire guards to watch the lot, and car owners can request that their vehicles be driven to the office. It is also rumored that various car companies and gas stations are planning to build parking lots. The Municipal Council is also setting up a free parking lot between Jiujiang Road and Beijing Road, which can accommodate 116 cars. This is the only free parking lot currently under construction in Shanghai. If needed in the future, it is planned to build another lot along the Suzhou Creek. In total, there will be three parking lots, although only one offers free parking, it can accommodate 300 vehicles. According to a report from the Police Department, after the implementation of the new parking regulations, 350 vehicles will no longer be able to park for free. However, the British-owned Public Bus Company claims that the number is closer to 500. Therefore, the company is drafting a protest against the Municipal Council's implementation of the new regulations.

According to Datong News Agency, two dredging buoys erected by the Shanghai Dredging Bureau at the Shentan Dredging Zone were lost due to the recent hurricane. Qianjiangzui Light Beacon on the Yangtze River Relit, Temporary Lightship Removed, Hydrographic Office Announcement Yesterday

The Shanghai Hydrographic Office issued Announcement No. 220 yesterday, stating that the "Qianjiangzui" light beacon on the Wuhu-Anqing section has been relit, and the temporary lightship has been removed. (1) The "Qianjiangzui" light beacon has been relit at a bearing of 276 degrees from the "Qianjiangkou" light beacon, at a distance of 8.1 chains (every 10 chains is equal to 1 nautical mile, 117 degrees 13 minutes east longitude, 30 degrees 32.1 minutes north latitude), abbreviated as two fixed red and white (vertical) double fixed lights, two lights hanging vertically, red on top and white on the bottom. Explanation: Water level is currently above 35 feet (Anqing water gauge). The above-mentioned light beacon is located in the above-mentioned direction and will be relit. (2) The temporary lightship has been removed at a bearing of 265 degrees from the "Qianjiangkou" light beacon, at a distance of 2.28 nautical miles, 117 degrees 21 minutes east longitude, and approximately 30 degrees 31 minutes north latitude. Explanation: The above-mentioned temporary lightship will be removed on the above-mentioned date. Related nautical charts: Ministry of the Navy Hydrographic Chart No. 158. Original reporting agency: Jianghan Customs River Patrol Office. Note: The directions in this shipping announcement are calculated from 0 degrees due north, turning clockwise to 359 degrees. However, the direction of the light is calculated from the sea. The range of the light is based on clear weather. The fog signal is only used in foggy weather. If necessary, further explanation will be provided. Depth measurements are based on the datum used in the largest-scale chart.

Inheritance Dispute Loses Third Appeal, Hu Seeks Revenge, Writes Threats and Throws Excrement, Hu Ji'an Suffers Intolerable Harassment

Hu Ganqing, a native of Hangzhou, Zhejiang, was extensively involved in business in Shanghai, including shares in Hu Qingyutang on Beijing Road, Fuchang Ginseng Shop in the South City, Zhang Yongchang Hardware Store on Wuhu Road, and Xinlisha Restaurant on Simalu Road. However, since Hu's death, all the stock certificates of the various stores and the residence at No. 132 Guling Road have been inherited and managed by his son, Hu Ji'an. Since then, the family has experienced many problems and incessant litigation. The son of a Mr. Li, a bookkeeper in the Hu residence, filed a lawsuit with the First Special District Court's Criminal Division last September 16 in the name of Hu Sheng, accusing Hu Ji'an of embezzlement, claiming that Hu Sheng was the adopted son of the late Hu Ganqing, who had been forced to live in Suzhou since the age of eight or nine, and that now that Ganqing had passed away, all the inheritance had been embezzled by Hu Ji'an. However, after the trial, Hu Sheng lost all three appeals, and the verdict was final. Unexpectedly, Hu Sheng refused to repent and, since May of last year, repeatedly pestered Hu Ji'an for loans. This year, he even wrote a threatening letter with harsh words and threats to Hu Ji'an's life. Hu Ji'an reported this to the Old Gate Police Station and requested that the First Special District Court issue an arrest warrant. On the night of the 18th of this month, Hu Sheng took a can of excrement to the door of Hu Ji'an's home at No. 132 Guling Road and threw it, and posted a notice on the door, declaring that the person throwing the excrement was your brother, in intimidating language. At 6:05 p.m. the day before yesterday, Hu Sheng went to the Xinlisha Restaurant on Guangxi Road, intending to make trouble, and was arrested by Chinese detectives Zhang Yuanjing, Li Shugui, Xue Youwen, etc., and taken to the Old Gate Police Station. Yesterday morning, they were handed over to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police Attorney Jiang Baoqi charged Hu Sheng with obstructing freedom under Article 305 of the Criminal Law. According to Hu Ji'an's complaint, the defendant Hu Sheng confessed that he had someone else write the threatening letter and that he had thrown the excrement. Judge Dai verified the confession and ordered the case to be adjourned until next Thursday for further hearing. The defendant was returned to police custody.

Lu Zhangde Sued by Siblings for Embezzling Inheritance, Investigation into Sale of Landed Property to be Made Through Registered Foreign Firm

Lu Zhangde, residing at No. 75 Jessfield Road, possesses substantial assets in inheritance. Recently, his brother Lu Zhangci and sister Lu Fengqin filed a lawsuit against him in the First Special District Court, accusing him of embezzling inheritance. According to the plaintiff's statement, their legal mother, Wu, being childless, adopted the son of her late husband Zhongfu's aunt, Wang (i.e., the defendant), as her heir. Subsequently, Zhongfu remarried Zhao, who was also childless, and then married Liu, who gave birth to Fengzhu, Zhangren, and Zhangliang. Then, he married Ding, who gave birth to the plaintiff siblings. During his lifetime, Zhongfu served as the manager of the real estate department of the British firm Telier & Co. for decades, accumulating substantial wealth. On November 14, 1926, Zhongfu passed away, leaving behind over 100,000 yuan in cash and a considerable amount of real estate. Initially, the defendant managed the assets, deciding to entrust the management of the real estate to the stepmother, Zhao. On October 7, 1931, Zhao passed away, and all the inheritance was managed entirely by the defendant. In January of this year, the defendant, having depleted the cash left by Zhongfu, proposed dividing the property and living separately, and insisted on receiving a larger share. The plaintiffs agreed to his proposal, and a division contract was signed. It was discovered that since Lu's property had been managed by the defendant, there had never been any public accounting of income and expenses. It was recently learned that among Zhongfu's inheritance was a plot of land of 3 mu, 5 fen, 2 li, and 4 hao located at the corner of Guiyang Road in Yangshupu, which the defendant had embezzled and pocketed the proceeds from. The defendant, being an adopted son, had no right to inherit according to the laws at the time. The plaintiffs were unwilling to engage in fraternal strife and had always tacitly acknowledged him as one of Lu's heirs. However, the defendant completely disregarded his conscience and arbitrarily embezzled the inheritance, constituting a crime under Article 335, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, they specially requested to be prosecuted. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Pan Zhenyang summoned the plaintiff Lu Zhangci, who explained the circumstances and stated that the defendant had secretly sold the real estate on Guiyang Road, which is now worth 70,000 yuan. Furthermore, it has been discovered that seven other titles to land have also been secretly sold. The plaintiffs submitted the title deeds and a ledger of the total title deeds to the court, requesting a thorough investigation. The defendant Lu Zhangde testified that the real estate was sold by Zhao and the other two mothers, and that he had never sold an inch of land after taking over the management. Judge Pan stated that the seller of the real estate should be investigated through the registered foreign firm to clarify the matter. He then adjourned the hearing until the afternoon of the 30th of this month.

Unregistered Smokers - Specially Allowed to Voluntarily Apply for Cessation - If Still Unrepentant... Investigation and Military Law Will Be Applied

Since the general inspection of smokers has ended, those unregistered smokers who voluntarily apply for cessation will be given special consideration. Those who remain unrepentant will be punished according to the law once discovered. Door-to-door inspections of smokers will be conducted, and each district will mobilize its personnel to begin. The details are as follows:

Special Permission for Cessation

The Municipal Public Security Bureau states that since the general inspection of smokers in this city ended on September 10th, there have been quite a few who have voluntarily applied for cessation. However, the Smoking Prohibition Regulations do not explicitly state whether to accept applications or impose penalties. Therefore, the Municipal Government specially requested the Military Commission's General Supervision Department for Smoking Prohibition to provide an interpretation. Afterwards, to give smokers a chance to repent and reform, smokers who have not registered but voluntarily apply for cessation will be given special consideration and will not be penalized. However, if they remain unrepentant, they will be punished according to military law once discovered, without leniency.

Mobilization for Inspection

After the completion of the procedures for smokers' household pledges and guarantees, the Municipal Public Security Bureau immediately ordered each district station to conduct door-to-door inspections based on the pledge forms filled out by each household. Each district station has already dispatched police to mobilize. If there are suspicious households with sallow complexions and blackened teeth, they will be questioned in detail. If it is confirmed that they are addicted and have not registered, they will be punished according to the law.

A Frugal Wedding

Mr. Feng Bingnan, a business magnate in Shanghai, held a wedding ceremony for his third son on the 10th of this month. To save money and time, Mr. Feng specifically stated three points in his invitation cards: first, he originally intended to decline all gifts, but if relatives and friends insisted on giving something, please send cash only, but each gift should not exceed ten yuan in national currency; second, there would be no wedding hall for the wedding ceremony, and congratulations would be declined; third, in addition to preparing refreshments on the afternoon of the auspicious day to entertain guests, there would be no separate banquet, and the funds saved from the banquet, together with the cash gifts from relatives and friends, would be donated to the Shanghai Renji Hospital and Sacred Heart Hospital for the purpose of helping the poor and sick. This approach not only reduces the various formalities of the wedding ceremony but also benefits the poor and sick. Therefore, although many guests gathered that afternoon and the road was crowded with carriages and horses, the order was well maintained and both the host and guests were happy. It was truly the simplest and most frugal wedding ceremony, which is worthy of emulation by the general public during this time of economic depression.

The 301st inspection was conducted at the bank's Issuing Bureau on September 19th of the 25th year of the Republic of China. The total amount of exchange coupon reserve is 30,786,4374 yuan, including 20,625,3674 yuan of cash reserve. This cash reserve includes 10,323,6730.49 yuan deposited in the bank's issuing headquarters, branches, and sub-branches, and 10,301,6943.51 yuan deposited with other banks. The guaranteed reserve is equivalent to 10,161,0700 yuan in silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange coupons issued is 400,9630.07 yuan. The total amount of customs gold exchange coupon reserve is 400,9630.07 yuan. This reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, valued at 51.68, totaling 400,9630.07 yuan in customs gold. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve should be at least 60%, and the remainder should be guaranteed by legal collateral. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guaranteed reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This report is hereby submitted." Aoshan is a common Mid-Autumn Festival decoration in Fujian, and Daxin Amusement Park is a pioneer in Shanghai.

Sports News

Our National Football Team: Detailed Account of Two Matches in England. Universal Praise from the Press; Great Surprise Among the British. From Lieshan, Sent from London.

London Airmail Special

The Chinese football team's participation in the World Games was initially seen as unfortunate, as they were drawn against England in their first match. In international sports competitions, we often encounter strong opponents right away. However, if we don't focus too much on immediate wins and losses, we can understand the significance of this Sino-British football match. This competition has laid the groundwork for the Chinese football team's standing in the international arena. The efforts of the Chinese football team, even though they resulted in a loss, are still our only achievement and gain in these World Games.

Speaking of football, it is the national sport of England. The English football team has always held a leading position internationally. When the news of the match between the Chinese and English teams was announced, the British public felt a sense of novelty. Not only do Chinese people know how to play football, but they have even sent a team to participate in the World Games. Usually, they only use the phrase "Chinese people playing football" as a joke. However, the British newspapers, knowing about our team's performance in Southeast Asia, seemed somewhat concerned, fearing an upset. Some newspapers even suggested that the Chinese team had the potential to "threaten" the "dignity" of the English team. Although our team lost 0-2, the audience and European newspapers unanimously praised our team's skills, with the sentiment "The Chinese team is also a first-class international amateur football team" being heard everywhere. In fact, we were not defeated.

An Introduction by a British Lady

During the Berlin competition, our team's performance was excellent, and our skills were no less than those of the English team. Unfortunately, we lost, which garnered extra sympathy from the audience. Among the audience was a Miss Smith, whose father is the leader of a British amateur football organization, Islington Corinthians. She voluntarily asked her father to arrange matches for our team in London. After several discussions, our team accepted the invitation and decided to play two matches in London against British amateur football teams: the first against the Corinthians team, and the second against the Casuals team, the British Amateur Football Champions.

The Chinese football team arrived in London on August 28th. The person who contributed the most to the reception from the overseas Chinese community was Mr. Zhang Sili, a staff member of the Chinese Association. On the British side, Mr. Smith was particularly enthusiastic. Although the Chinese team members had endured a long journey of four months and played thirty-five matches, with almost half of the team injured, everyone remained spirited and left an excellent impression. In addition to publishing photos of our team members, British newspapers often featured special articles introducing our team's combat capabilities. The "King of Football," Mr. Li Huitang, seemed older than before. After these months of travel, his face showed fatigue. Little Blackie, Chen Zhenhe, lost a lot of weight, probably because he always gives his all in every game. Naturally, this is not surprising, as he suffered from the hardships of travel and the football field. Even Sun Shunjun did not look like a fat person anymore, let alone others. The one in the best spirits was Tan Jiangbai. One look at Tan's physique and you know he should be a football star, but when you talk to him, he is very cultured.

When asked about whether he was used to "European life," Little Blackie said, "I haven't had Chinese food for months and have been eating Western food all day. It's been terrible. I'd rather go back sooner rather than later." Xu Yahui said that he started missing home after two months abroad and wants to return to China as soon as possible. This is almost the motto of the entire team.

One of the team members told the reporter about his views on the Chinese team's skills. He said, "We didn't learn to play football from any teacher. We just watch how others play and steal the good moves." The English Post reported that this team seemed to be stronger than the British team that competed in Berlin.

Before the match, a military band played the national anthems of China and England. Amidst the enthusiastic welcome of 15,000 spectators, the Chinese team took the offensive after the English team kicked off. Our team's skills were high and our teamwork was skillful. We dominated the first half and won a lot of applause. Within five minutes of the start, Feng Jingxiang scored the first goal. Within twenty minutes, Li Huitang received a pass from Chen Zhenhe and, under the watch of the English inner defense, Li still kicked a long shot, and our team scored two goals in a row. Li's kick was clear and beautiful, as if he shot without effort. The applause on the field thundered. A reporter from the British News Summary praised Li's goal as one of the best he had seen in years. The English team counterattacked but was blocked by Huang Jiliang and gained nothing. At thirty minutes, Chen Zhenhe crossed the ball in front of the English goal. The English goalkeeper rushed to save and fell to the ground. The ball was in front of an empty goal, but unfortunately, Feng Jingxiang was one step late and missed a good opportunity. After that, the momentum of the English team suddenly increased, and the Chinese goal was almost completely surrounded. Huang Jiliang was bold, careful, quick, and caught all the high and low balls, leaving the English forwards with no room to develop, until the English midfielder headed in a goal from a corner kick near the end of the first half.

At the start of the second half, the English team relied on its strong physique and seemed to be getting stronger. Our team was already at a disadvantage due to being tired. In addition, players such as Tan Jiang, Huang Jiliang, etc., were injured and barely able to play. In fact, they were not fully recovered, so it was impossible to compare them with professional football teams. I asked him if the team leader gave instructions from the sidelines during the game, and if there was a fixed formation. He said no, we mostly fight on our own and improvise. This may be the reason why the Chinese team failed to make further progress. However, Dr. Rong Qizhao said that after returning to China, he plans to suggest to the Sports Association that they hire an English football coach to come to China. We hope that his plan can be realized soon, and that perhaps in four years, the Chinese football team will have the opportunity to make the Chinese flag fly at the World Games.

Against the Corinthians team, time: August 31st, 6:30 PM, location: Highbury Football Stadium, London. As a result, our team lost 2-3. In the first half, 1-1, our team won. Goal scorers: Li Huitang 1, Feng Jingxiang 1. Our team's formation that day was as follows:

This English team is called the Corinthians team, but in reality, it is a collection of elites from various amateur football teams, plus naval and army soldiers. The whole team's spirit was not as good as in the first half. The English team was indeed superior to our team at this point. Fortunately, goalkeeper Huang Jiliang has made amazing progress in recent days, remaining calm and saving several dangerous shots that seemed impossible to save. Once, an English forward dribbled the ball close to the Chinese goal. It seemed that there was little hope, but the goalkeeper Huang had the courage to surprise the opponent, take the opportunity to jump out and fall to the ground, and the ball was forced into a corner kick. Huang Jiliang was the hero of the Chinese team that day. Every time he saved a ball, the audience gave him a burst of warm applause. The British Daily Express said that Huang Jiliang is the star of the Chinese team, and his saves won the hearts of the audience. The News Summary said that the Chinese goalkeeper is a substitute, but his saving skills and agility are no less than the best goalkeepers in the British football team. The Daily Herald said that Huang Jiliang saved so many dangerous balls, and he is still a substitute, so the wonderful skills of the Chinese official goalkeeper can be imagined. Although this is the case, in the twenty minutes before the end of the game, the English forwards successively scored two goals, making the score 3-2. Our team failed. The inside defenders of our team were very good. Cai Wenli and Xu Yahui worked especially hard.

Forward Little Blackie ran fast and did not give way to the British, creating many opportunities to shoot, and was our team's only robot.

After the game, our team members were warmly welcomed by the spectators in the stadium, because they were able to understand the true ability of the Chinese team. When we walked out of the stadium, we still heard the audience greeting the overseas Chinese everywhere: "This was a really good kick!" This is our harvest.

The next day, British newspapers praised our team's performance, with the Daily Mail saying that the names of the Chinese team members are a mystery, but their football playing is not difficult to understand at all. The Daily Express said that the Chinese played a very authentic game of football. The Daily Herald said, "The Chinese team's technique is better than the British team, and their failure is due to bad luck." What more could we ask for? In terms of skills, our team's individual techniques have reached the top level. However, there are also shortcomings: first, the team members are too tired and lack energy. Not only can they not outrun others in the field, but in the last ten or twenty minutes, they can hardly move themselves. The reason for losing the ball lies here, because European football games last for ninety minutes, which is twenty minutes longer than Chinese football games. Secondly, the teamwork is not good enough, and there is no predetermined line of attack. In particular, the communication between the forwards is not smooth, so often after the forward gets the ball, they either pass it to an empty spot, or they have to stand and see where their teammates are, and thus repeatedly lose good shooting opportunities. On the contrary, the English team forwards pass to each other without hesitation as soon as they get the ball, and immediately reach our team's second line of defense. Third, due to physical reasons, their kicking strength is not strong enough, and the forwards' shots are weak. As for tackling the ball, it seems that they are still not as good as the English team. However, the Chinese people are smart and quick-thinking, so many wonderful balls are unexpected by the enemy. This is our team's strength, and it also relies on personal talent, which cannot be learned through hard work.

In addition, there are two other points where the Chinese football team has brought glory to the country. After the Berlin game, the German newspapers praised the elegant behavior of both Chinese and English players during the Sino-British football match, which was in line with the spirit of sportsmen in every way, and was the most ideal match in the World Games, which could be used as a model for everyone. After the London game, the Daily Mail also specifically praised our team for this point: the Chinese team members only kick the ball and do not kick people. This is something we feel we can be very proud of to the world. Another point is that most European newspapers have published the backgrounds of the team members, including doctors, businessmen, officers, policemen, martial artists, students, and all kinds of people in society. This is enough to prove the popularity of football in China. In fact, most of what we hoped for has been achieved. The Chinese football team's trip is only missing a victory in name.

Central China Games: Number of Athletes from Each Province

Changsha, 23rd – According to telegrams from various provinces regarding the athletes for the Central China Games, Hunan and Jiangxi will each send 200 athletes, Anhui will send 100, and Hubei will send 180.

Municipal Games: Item Registration the Day After Tomorrow

The fourth Shanghai Municipal Games, organized by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, are scheduled to be held at the Municipal Central Sports Field for three days starting October 22nd. It is divided into four groups: Open, University, Sports School, and Middle School. The Open and University groups are each divided into men's and women's divisions, while the Middle School group is divided into senior high, junior high, men's, and women's divisions. The Sports School group is divided into Physical Education Specialization and Physical Education Teacher Training, with men's and women's divisions. Registration for participation in events by various schools will begin from the 26th to the 28th of this month. In track and field, each athlete can register for multiple events. Except for relay races, the Open, University, and Sports School groups are limited to four events for both men and women, while the Middle School group is limited to three events for both men and women. In the University, Middle School, and Sports School groups, each school is limited to four participants per event per group. Four places are awarded for each event, with scores calculated as 5-3-2-1. Track and field team championships are awarded to the University, Middle School, and Sports School groups, with separate men's and women's championships. The unit with the highest score wins the championship. The three units with the next highest scores win the second, third, and fourth places, respectively. If two or more units have the same score, the unit with the most first-place finishes in various events is judged to be the winner, and so on. The events and eligibility for each group have been published in various newspapers. Each person is limited to four items in martial arts competitions.

Education News

Zhejiang Cultural Relics Exhibition: Exhibition Period to Open in Hangzhou on October 26; Ningbo, Shaoxing, and Taizhou Collection Branches Send Exhibits

The Zhejiang Provincial Department of Education has ordered the Zhejiang Cultural Relics Exhibition to be organized by the Provincial Library. Preparations are underway, and collection branches have been set up in Beijing and Shanghai. The news has been published in this newspaper. It is now known that the association was originally scheduled to open on October 10th, but due to the impact of the summer heat on the preparation and collection, it was unable to complete on schedule. In addition, the National Assembly representatives elections held in various provincial regions have further delayed the collection work. Therefore, the Standing Committee members of the association's Design Committee, Wang Tingyang and Yu Yueyuan, sent a public letter to the Provincial Department of Education requesting an extension of the deadline, which has been approved by the department. It has been decided to postpone it to October 26th, and it will still open at the Provincial Library on Hangzhou Daxue Road. Currently, nine administrative supervision districts within Zhejiang Province have established collection branches. Yinxian, Shaoxing, Jiaxing, Taizhou, Yongjia, JiaShan, Yuhang and other places are also following provincial orders to prepare to open local cultural relic exhibitions, some of which have already been held or will be held soon. After the exhibition, they will select and send the exhibits to the province. It is said that Ningbo, Shaoxing, WenZhou, and Jiaxing have collected a lot. The existing local chronicles and enrollment records of Fan's Tianyi Pavilion in Ningbo have also been borrowed with the consent of the Fan family. The Liu family's Jiaye Building in Nanxun has a rich collection of books, among which the manuscripts and rare editions of Zhejiang sages will be sent for collection. The association has contacted various collectors in Hangzhou and is ready. It is expected that the books on display will be very impressive. The association's Executive Committee held its third meeting the day before yesterday (19th), and it is also heard that a Standing Committee meeting of the Design Committee is planned to be held within a week. After the Shanghai Collection Branch was established on the 11th, the Zhejiang Department of Education added Mr. Ye Gongchao as the director of the branch, and Mr. Zhang Shouchong and Qin Runqing as the deputy directors, and designated Ningbo Road Fuyuan Qianzhuang as the venue. It has now started to collect items. Collectors from all walks of life can write to the bank to request the method and registration form for solicitation, and send them to Hangzhou for compilation. The association will be responsible for returning them after the exhibition.

Provincial and Municipal Schools and Libraries Installed Radio Statistics: A Total of 855 Sets, Jiangsu Province Has the Most

In order to enable secondary schools and people's education centers in various provinces and cities to universally install radios, so as to enhance the effectiveness of radio broadcasting education, the Ministry of Education promulgated the General Outline of Methods for Installing Radios in Secondary Schools and Public Education Centers Nationwide in June of the 24th year [of the Republic, i.e., 1935]. According to Item 3 of the Outline, secondary schools should complete installation by the end of December of this year, and public education centers should complete installation by the end of June of the 26th year [1937]. The purchase of these wireless radios was entirely arranged by the Ministry with electrical manufacturers, to be paid for on schedule and distributed by the Ministry to the responsible education departments in each province and city for installation in schools and libraries. As for the price of the radios, it was originally supposed to be raised by each province and city, and paid on schedule. However, considering the financial difficulties of schools and libraries in various provinces and cities, the Ministry has carefully considered local conditions and provided appropriate subsidies for the purchase of machines. In the 24th year, the Ministry subsidized the full price for remote provinces, and a half of the price for inland provinces and cities. Subsidies will also be provided in the current year according to local conditions. It is also heard that the price of machines this year is much lower than before, with a DC machine costing 102 yuan and an AC machine costing 80 yuan. It is also learned that, in order to understand the installation situation in various provinces and cities, the Ministry has completed the investigation of the situation of self-installed radios in schools and libraries in various provinces and cities before the 24th year, the installation of radios in schools and libraries in various provinces and cities in the 24th year, and the planned installation of radios in the 25th year [1936]. The statistical results of the investigation are recorded below: (A) Before the 24th year, schools and libraries in various provinces and cities self-installed a total of 855 radios, including 208 in Jiangsu Province, 78 in Zhejiang Province, 77 in Anhui Province, 19 in Jiangxi Province, 38 in Hubei Province, 3 in Hunan Province, 34 in Sichuan Province, 58 in Shandong Province, 2 in Hebei Province, 3 in Tianjin City, 53 in Henan Province, 15 in Shanxi Province, 1 in Shaanxi Province, 2 in Fujian Province, 49 in Guangdong Province, 7 in Guangxi Province, 4 in Yunnan Province, 11 in Chahar Province, 9 in Suiyuan Province, 17 in Nanjing City, 29 in Shanghai City, 10 in Qingdao City, 29 in Beiping City, and 1 in Weihaiwei. (B) In the 24th year, schools and libraries in various provinces and cities installed a total of 810 radios, including some in Jiangsu Province, 34 in Zhejiang Province, some in Jiangxi Province, 62 in Anhui Province, 88 in Hunan Province, 37 in Hubei Province, 36 in Sichuan Province, 128 in Shandong Province, 8 in Hebei Province, 34 in Shanxi Province, 17 in Shaanxi Province, 41 in Gansu Province, 121 in Fujian Province, 3 in Guangdong Province, 52 in Guangxi Province, 16 in Guangzhou Province, 20 in Yunnan Province, 25 in Chahar Province, 8 in Suiyuan Province, 7 in Ningxia Province, 8 in Xinjiang, 3 in Shanghai City, 21 in Beiping City, 3 in Qingdao City, and 2 in Weihaiwei. (C) In the 25th year, schools and libraries in various provinces and cities plan to install a total of 783 radios, including 98 in Zhejiang Province, 27 in Anhui Province, 2 in Jiangxi Province, 9 in Hubei Province, 93 in Hunan Province, 32 in Shandong Province, 91 in Hebei Province (including 2 in Tianjin City), 135 in Henan Province, 7 in Shanxi Province, 33 in Shaanxi Province, 2 in Gansu Province, 13 in Fujian Province, 140 in Guangdong Province, 2 in Guangxi Province, 11 in Chahar Province, 6 in Suiyuan Province, 23 in Qinghai Province, 26 in Shanghai City, 11 in Beiping City, 2 in Qingdao City, and 2 in Weihaiwei City. It is said that Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Xinjiang and other provinces have not yet submitted reports.

Ministry of Education Compiles and Prints Social Education Reading Materials

(Nanjing, 23rd dispatch) In order to promote social education, the Ministry of Education is intensifying its efforts in film broadcasting and the implementation of public supplementary education, as well as preparing to reorganize libraries, museums, and other social education undertakings. It is reported that, in addition to improving public reading materials, the Ministry is currently dividing them into two categories: primary school textbooks and supplementary reading materials. The first four volumes of primary textbooks are expected to be compiled by mid-October, and the advanced part will be compiled within this year. In addition, teaching materials for music, self-defense, and other subjects will be compiled by experts within the year. As for supplementary materials, in addition to the Ministry's investigation, various provinces and cities can compile and print them themselves. The Ministry has also decided to compile a "Public Common Knowledge Treasury" book, with 100 types to be completed within the 26th year [1937]. In addition, correspondence reading materials, such as dramas, stories, songbooks, and storytelling, will be entrusted to the Beiping Correspondence Reading Material Compilation and Publishing House for compilation and editing.

Exchange Students Between China and Germany: Three of the Four German Students Arrive in Beiping; Tsinghua University to Send Five Students This Year

(Reuters, Beiping, 23rd dispatch) The German Far East Cultural Association has sent four exchange students to Tsinghua University in Beiping. Among them, Mr. Ulville Wider, Mr. Shellmeyer, and Ms. Hildeberlinde, departed from Berlin on the 8th of this month and arrived in China via Northwestern Siberia. It is reported that they intend to study Chinese law, history, and geology, respectively. Another person was originally planning to come with them, but was delayed due to illness. As for Tsinghua University, it also intends to send five exchange students to Germany this year. There are currently 15 applicants, and the school authorities will announce the selection results after the selection is decided.

This Year's Students Studying in the United States Have Enrolled Separately

Mr. Zhu Shaoping, the General Director of the World Chinese Student Association at 191 Carter Road, received a letter yesterday from Mr. Lu Shiyin, the Chinese Consul in Seattle, stating that most of the students who came to the United States this summer have arrived safely in the United States and have enrolled in classes. The excerpt from the letter is as follows: "Mr. ShaoPing, Upon receiving your letter, I was pleased to learn that the students are arriving in the United States in stages. In addition to formally notifying the Immigration Bureau and Customs as usual, I personally went to the port to take care of the students upon arrival. There have been no problems with student landings in the past two years, which is comforting. Fifty-seven students arrived in Seattle on the 2nd of this month. I contacted various organizations in advance, and they hosted a banquet on the evening of the 2nd to welcome them. The next day, cars were arranged to tour the scenic spots. The students have now traveled east in different directions. Before the next group of students comes to the United States, I hope you can instruct them not to neglect etiquette in the dining hall. Sincerely, Lu Shiyin, September 5, 25th year."

Yarn and Cotton: Buyers Purchase Yarn for This Month, Revitalizing the Yarn Market; Several Hundred Bales of Yarn Also Stored in Warehouses

The yarn market is trending upwards. Initially, buyers were purchasing yarn for this month and storing several hundred bales of yarn in warehouses, which made the market increasingly tight. At the same time, the spot yarn sales were brisk, with buyers from Sichuan, the inland, Guangdong, Changsha, and other regions purchasing in succession, further strengthening the upward trend. It eased slightly in the afternoon, but the industry still absorbed the yarns sold for hedging. The last transaction was at 201.7 yuan, which was 4.3 yuan higher than the price of last month.

Yarn for This Month is Even Tighter: At the opening of the bidding yarn market, all months showed a consistent rise, and the market sentiment was even better on the last day of trading for this month's yarn. This was because buyers were purchasing yarn for this month, especially yarn for warehouse storage, as the factories lacked spot goods and the prices were relatively low. As a result, the upward trend became even stronger, and the forward months were also affected. Market prices rose step by step, but Deda, Hengyi, Jinchang, Mingde, Wangtai, Xingxie, and Fukang sold, while Yuda, Tongji, Yiji, Hexing, Senkang, Dianji, and Dachang bought in large quantities. The result of the bidding yarn was that this month rose by 1.9 yuan compared to the closing price of the previous day, and the forward months rose by 0.8-0.9 yuan. At the opening in the afternoon, the market situation for this month was slightly flat, as some people sold off their stagnant goods. Although there were buyers, they were still hesitant, and the forward months also fell by 0.3-0.4 yuan. By the close of the market, some people in the industry bought in, and it was heard that spot yarn transactions were still over 3,000 bales, and the price rose again by 0.3-0.4 yuan. As a result, this month fell by 0.7 yuan compared to the closing price in the morning, and the rest fell by 0.2-0.4 yuan. It was found that Deda sold 2,050 bales, Hengyi 1 bale, Changfeng 1,510 bales, Xingxie 3,250 bales, Fukang 2,400 bales, Renfeng 1,100 bales, and Xincheng 1,350 bales. Xingchang bought 1,000 bales, Gengfeng 1,250 bales, Juxing 1,200 bales, Tongji 2,100 bales, Yuda 4,700 bales, Dafeng 2,700 bales, Zhenda 1,450 bales, Yiji 1,450 bales, Senkang 3,650 bales, Shenji 1,700 bales, Taichang 1,000 bales, and Dachang 1,000 bales. Cotton Market Subjected to Pressure After the Rise

The cotton market is quiet. Because the yarn market is lively, factories have a strong need for raw cotton, and the market prices in various producing areas are firm, and people's hearts are good. However, general non-industry people are constantly tending to abandon it due to the pressure of 70,000 dan of coarse velvet cotton. However, the situation of spot cotton is excellent.

Bidding Cotton Rises and Falls Normally: At the opening of the bidding cotton market, American cotton rose slightly by half a pound. After the second transaction, due to the rise in the yarn market, factories actually purchased raw materials, and the selling price in the local area was not relaxed, and the buying interest suddenly rose. Changhe, which had thrown the largest amount of empty positions the previous day, also came to buy in. The market price rose step by step. It was found that Mingde, Hexing, Shenji, Dachang, Shengyuan, Fukang, and other firms sold, while Yuda and Changhe made up for a lot. As a result, the prices for each month increased by 1.5 to 2 cents compared to the closing price of the previous day. At the opening in the afternoon, the market was calm, up and down by 5 cents. There was still no change in the second and third transactions. By the close of the market, it turned tight and returned by a small amount of 5 to 10 cents. As a result, the prices for each month fell by 10 cents compared to the closing price in the morning. American Cotton Rises Back Due to Short Covering — Indian and English Cotton Still Depressed —

Yesterday, the American cotton market opened, and the market was flat and tired. Each month fell by three pounds or rose by one pound. At the beginning of the morning, the October issue had continued to close positions, and cotton farmers were hedging sales. Then, domestic industry, Liverpool, and New Orleans bought in, hedging sales decreased, and brokers bought in on the dips. The market price rose back. There were not many off-market transactions, but the increase in world consumption was quite noticeable, and the spot demand was active and the foot was strong. At the closing, it rose due to short covering and domestic industry buying in. It is estimated that the spot price rose by 7 pounds and the futures price rose by 4 to 8 pounds. English cotton spot price fell by 11 points and futures price fell by 4 to 9 points. Indian cotton brokers bought Belaraki and sold Omla. Later, cotton merchants had a slight cross-transaction. It is estimated that Pingleer fell by 1.25 Roby. The original telegram is recorded on the left (22nd dispatch):

Finance

Pure Gold Has Concerns of Falling Back; Specie Buyers Wait and See

Yesterday's gold market saw a decline in buying interest due to a strengthening exchange rate trend and general apprehension about a potential pullback in pure gold prices. As a result, prices retreated by four jiao. Initially, the overseas silver market saw British prices rise and American prices remain stable. There were rumors of "Big Foot" positions selling off after the market closed at listed prices, indicating a weakening market. The forward silver price in Monte Video remained unchanged, with a premium of three and a half li. The exchange rate continued to strengthen, and the price of raw gold in London rose by half a penny. The Central Bank's listed rates were released, showing no change in British and American rates, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The listed price for standard gold specie rose to 27.1 yuan. Pre-market trading opened at around 24 yuan, but lacked support due to the rising exchange rate and fears of a decline in raw gold prices. Chun Hui Yong and other firms offered spot sales, opening slightly lower and initially weakening before stabilizing. Major players took advantage of the lower prices to buy, gradually pushing prices back up. However, sellers offered supply at higher prices, and major players also unloaded positions. The HSBC exchange rate listing showed that both British and American rates had fallen back to their previous levels. When the silver equalization tax was announced, it rose by half a fen, leading to a slight increase in trading. However, due to a large number of players taking advantage of the higher prices, there was continued selling pressure, making it difficult for prices to rise further. As a result, the trend at midday was peaceful, but with much struggle. Yesterday, the swap rate was quoted by the long side at 2.8 yuan. The following is a record of the market situation for the first half of the day:

The market opened this morning at 1123.6 yuan, four jiao lower than the previous closing price. Chun Yuan Yong sold off, falling 3.4 yuan. Heng Yu, Sheng Yuan Yong, Da De Cheng and others bought heavily, rising to 4 yuan. Yuan Heng, Qia Feng Yong, and others sold off, retreating to 3.6 yuan. The HSBC exchange rate listing showed no change in British and American rates, and the silver equalization tax rose by half a fen. There was some struggle in the middle of the day. Fu Xing Yong, Jin Feng Yong, Qing Fa Yong, and others took advantage of the lower prices to buy heavily, rising to 3.9 yuan. Yuan Mao Yong continued to sell, and retreated again to 3.6 yuan. Finally, although Qing Fa Yong and others advanced, Tong Tai Chang and others supplied, leading to a struggle. At noon, the market closed at 1123.6 yuan.

The closing price, based on the Central Bank's listed price for standard gold, rose to 1117.1 yuan. According to the closing price, it rose by about 6 yuan. The ledger prices for this month are 1118 yuan, October 1121 yuan, and November 1124 yuan. The spot market was stable, with Tianjin goods quoted at 9.75 yuan. Cooked red gold was selling at 11.5 yuan and buying at 7.5 yuan, with few counterparts. The ten-eleven month spread was quoted by Da Feng Heng to Chun Yuan Yong at 210 lots, Yi Yu at 14 lots, at 2.8 yuan.

Trading within the market was relatively peaceful. In summary, Jin Feng Yong, Heng Yu, Qing Fa Yong, Da De Cheng, Sheng Yuan Yong and others were on the buying side, while Tong Tai Chang, Shen Da Yong, Chun Yuan Yong, Xiang Feng, Qia Feng Yong, Fu Xing Yong, Yuan Heng and others were on the selling side.

The market situation for the first half of the day was peaceful, with the opening and closing prices both at 1123.6 yuan. The highest price was 1124 yuan, and the lowest price was 1123.4 yuan, with a range of six jiao. As a result, the market retreated four jiao compared to the previous closing price. There are still 595 gold bars remaining for this month, with a total of eight long positions and five short positions. The total number of transactions for the first half of the day was 1316 gold bars.

There are still 994 gold bars remaining from the October period that have not been swapped, with eleven long positions and eleven short positions.

The positions for the November period are as follows: Long positions include Fu Xing Yong with over 1000 lots, Heng Chang Yong with over 800, Wan Xing with over 700, Da Chang Xiang and Yuan Mao Yong with over 600 each, Wu Chang Xiang with over 400, Shen Kang with over 300, and Shun Li, Jin Feng Yong, and Qing Fa Yong with over 100 each. Short positions include Nei Feng Heng with over 1500 lots, Chun Yuan Yong with over 1100, Sheng Yuan Yong with over 700, Da De Cheng with over 500, Jing Fu with over 400, Gan Chang Xiang, Yuan Chang Yong, and Cheng Da with over 300 each, Yi Yu with over 200, Fu Tai Yong, Run Chang, Yu Fu Tai Heng, Tong Tai Chang, Shen Da Yong, Yong Jiu, Da Xiang He with over 100 each. The total number of lots is 7308, with a total of 30 long positions and 39 short positions.

Currency Exchange: Although the US Dollar is Loose, It Can Still Be Maintained

Yesterday's currency market saw a rise in exchange rates, with British currency tight and the US dollar loose, leading to a significant number of settlements. Early in the morning, overseas telegrams reported that London "big foot" positions, both near and far, rose by 0.0625. It was said that after the market closed, there were sellers offering at the listed price, indicating a weakening market. The New York silver market remained unchanged, and the Monte Video forward silver price remained unchanged, with a premium of three and a half li. The price of raw gold in London rose by half a penny. The British rate against the US dollar rose by half a point, the British rate against the French franc rose by six pounds, the US dollar against the British pound rose strongly by seventy-five points, and the US dollar against the French franc remained unchanged. The Central Bank's listed rates were released, showing no change in British and American rates, and the customs gold unit remained unchanged. The opening selling prices for the near-term market were 1 shilling, 2 pence, 0.25 and 0.3125 for British currency, and 30.1875 yuan for US currency. Compared to the previous close, the British rate was slightly tighter, while the US dollar was looser by 0.03125. After the opening, bank spreads varied, with occasional swaps. The HSBC exchange rate listing showed that both British and American rates remained unchanged and fluctuated. After the silver equalization tax was announced, it rose by half a fen. Foreign firms and Mobil were buying US dollars, and banks were happy to trade against them. The process was still struggling. Until noon, the selling prices for the near-term market were 1 shilling, 2 pence, 0.25 and 0.3125 for British currency, and 30.1875 yuan for US currency. Compared to the previous close, the British rate was slightly softer, while the US dollar was harder by 0.03125. The forward market was the same. Chinese merchants were watching from the sidelines, and banks were trading against each other. Foreign firms had a relatively large number of settlements. The following is a record of the transactions for the first half of the day:

The opening selling price for British currency this morning was 1 shilling, 2 pence, 0.28125. Hua Bi bought October at 0.28125. Mai Jia Li sold October's first half of the month at the inside price, and bought December at 0.21875. Zheng Jin bought January at the same price. Mai Jia Li sold to Zhong Xing October at 0.25. Shanghai sold January at 0.1875. You Li bought the first half of January at 0.1875 and 0.25 against each other. The closing selling prices were 1 shilling, 2 pence, 0.25 and 0.3125 for spot, 0.21875 and 0.25 for October, 0.21875 for November, and 0.1875 and 0.21875 for December. The buying prices were slightly higher.

The opening selling price for US currency this morning was 30.1875 yuan. Hua Bi sold to foreign firms December at 30 yuan, and February at 29.875 and 29.9375 against each other. He Lan sold to Mobil the first half of March at 29.8125. Shanghai sold to Mitsui spot at 30.1875 yuan. Hua Qi sold to Xin Feng April at 29 yuan, goods at 30.1875 yuan.
